sn35.1:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ.
sn35.1:1.2 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.
sn35.1:1.3 Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi:
sn35.1:1.4 “bhikkhavo”ti.
sn35.1:1.5 “Bhadante”ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn35.1:1.6 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn35.1:2.1 “Cakkhuṁ, bhikkhave, aniccaṁ.
sn35.1:2.2 Yadaniccaṁ taṁ dukkhaṁ;
sn35.1:2.3 yaṁ dukkhaṁ tadanattā.
sn35.1:2.4 Yadanattā taṁ ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti evametaṁ yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya daṭṭhabbaṁ.
sn35.1:2.5 Sotaṁ aniccaṁ.
sn35.1:2.6 Yadaniccaṁ …pe…
sn35.1:2.7 ghānaṁ aniccaṁ.
sn35.1:2.8 Yadaniccaṁ …pe…
sn35.1:2.9 jivhā aniccā.
sn35.1:2.10 Yadaniccaṁ taṁ dukkhaṁ;
sn35.1:2.11 yaṁ dukkhaṁ tadanattā.
sn35.1:2.12 Yadanattā taṁ ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti evametaṁ yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya daṭṭhabbaṁ.
sn35.1:2.13 Kāyo anicco.
sn35.1:2.14 Yadaniccaṁ …pe…
sn35.1:2.15 mano anicco.
sn35.1:2.16 Yadaniccaṁ taṁ dukkhaṁ;
sn35.1:2.17 yaṁ dukkhaṁ tadanattā.
sn35.1:2.18 Yadanattā taṁ ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti evametaṁ yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya daṭṭhabbaṁ.
sn35.1:2.19 Evaṁ passaṁ, bhikkhave, sutavā ariyasāvako cakkhusmimpi nibbindati, sotasmimpi nibbindati, ghānasmimpi nibbindati, jivhāyapi nibbindati, kāyasmimpi nibbindati, manasmimpi nibbindati.
sn35.1:2.20 Nibbindaṁ virajjati; virāgā vimuccati; vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti.
sn35.1:2.21 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.

sn35.13:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.13
sn35.13:0.2 2. Yamakavagga
sn35.13:0.3 Paṭhamapubbesambodhasutta
sn35.13:1.1 Sāvatthinidānaṁ.
sn35.13:1.2 “Pubbeva me, bhikkhave, sambodhā anabhisambuddhassa bodhisattasseva sato etadahosi:
sn35.13:1.3 ‘ko nu kho cakkhussa assādo, ko ādīnavo, kiṁ nissaraṇaṁ?
sn35.13:1.4 Ko sotassa …pe…
sn35.13:1.5 ko ghānassa …
sn35.13:1.6 ko jivhāya …
sn35.13:1.7 ko kāyassa …
sn35.13:1.8 ko manassa assādo, ko ādīnavo, kiṁ nissaraṇan’ti?
sn35.13:1.9 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi:
sn35.13:1.10 ‘yaṁ kho cakkhuṁ paṭicca uppajjati sukhaṁ somanassaṁ, ayaṁ cakkhussa assādo.
sn35.13:1.11 Yaṁ cakkhuṁ aniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, ayaṁ cakkhussa ādīnavo.
sn35.13:1.12 Yo cakkhusmiṁ chandarāgavinayo chandarāgappahānaṁ, idaṁ cakkhussa nissaraṇaṁ.
sn35.13:1.13 Yaṁ sotaṁ …pe…
sn35.13:1.14 yaṁ ghānaṁ …pe…
sn35.13:1.15 yaṁ jivhaṁ paṭicca uppajjati sukhaṁ somanassaṁ, ayaṁ jivhāya assādo.
sn35.13:1.16 Yaṁ jivhā aniccā dukkhā vipariṇāmadhammā, ayaṁ jivhāya ādīnavo.
sn35.13:1.17 Yo jivhāya chandarāgavinayo chandarāgappahānaṁ, idaṁ jivhāya nissaraṇaṁ.
sn35.13:1.18 Yaṁ kāyaṁ …pe…
sn35.13:1.19 yaṁ manaṁ paṭicca uppajjati sukhaṁ somanassaṁ, ayaṁ manassa assādo.
sn35.13:1.20 Yaṁ mano anicco dukkho vipariṇāmadhammo, ayaṁ manassa ādīnavo.
sn35.13:1.21 Yo manasmiṁ chandarāgavinayo chandarāgappahānaṁ, idaṁ manassa nissaraṇan’ti.
sn35.13:2.1 Yāvakīvañcāhaṁ, bhikkhave, imesaṁ channaṁ ajjhattikānaṁ āyatanānaṁ evaṁ assādañca assādato, ādīnavañca ādīnavato, nissaraṇañca nissaraṇato yathābhūtaṁ nābbhaññāsiṁ, neva tāvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya ‘anuttaraṁ sammāsambodhiṁ abhisambuddho’ti paccaññāsiṁ.
sn35.13:2.2 Yato ca khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, imesaṁ channaṁ ajjhattikānaṁ āyatanānaṁ evaṁ assādañca assādato, ādīnavañca ādīnavato, nissaraṇañca nissaraṇato yathābhūtaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ, athāhaṁ, bhikkhave, sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya ‘anuttaraṁ sammāsambodhiṁ abhisambuddho’ti paccaññāsiṁ.
sn35.13:2.3 Ñāṇañca pana me dassanaṁ udapādi:
sn35.13:2.4 ‘akuppā me vimutti, ayamantimā jāti, natthi dāni punabbhavo’”ti.
sn35.13:2.5 Paṭhamaṁ. "

sn35.14:1.4 ko gandhānaṁ …
sn35.14:1.5 ko rasānaṁ …
sn35.14:1.6 ko phoṭṭhabbānaṁ …
sn35.14:1.7 ko dhammānaṁ assādo, ko ādīnavo, kiṁ nissaraṇan’ti?
sn35.14:1.8 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi:
sn35.14:1.9 ‘yaṁ kho rūpe paṭicca uppajjati sukhaṁ somanassaṁ, ayaṁ rūpānaṁ assādo.
sn35.14:1.10 Yaṁ rūpā aniccā dukkhā vipariṇāmadhammā, ayaṁ rūpānaṁ ādīnavo.
sn35.14:1.11 Yo rūpesu chandarāgavinayo chandarāgappahānaṁ, idaṁ rūpānaṁ nissaraṇaṁ.
sn35.14:1.12 Yaṁ sadde …
sn35.14:1.13 gandhe …
sn35.14:1.14 rase …
sn35.14:1.15 phoṭṭhabbe …
sn35.14:1.16 yaṁ dhamme paṭicca uppajjati sukhaṁ somanassaṁ, ayaṁ dhammānaṁ assādo.
sn35.14:1.17 Yaṁ dhammā aniccā dukkhā vipariṇāmadhammā, ayaṁ dhammānaṁ ādīnavo.
sn35.14:1.18 Yo dhammesu chandarāgavinayo chandarāgappahānaṁ, idaṁ dhammānaṁ nissaraṇan’ti.
sn35.14:2.1 Yāvakīvañcāhaṁ, bhikkhave, imesaṁ channaṁ bāhirānaṁ āyatanānaṁ evaṁ assādañca assādato, ādīnavañca ādīnavato, nissaraṇañca nissaraṇato yathābhūtaṁ nābbhaññāsiṁ, neva tāvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya ‘anuttaraṁ sammāsambodhiṁ abhisambuddho’ti paccaññāsiṁ.
sn35.14:2.2 Yato ca khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, imesaṁ channaṁ bāhirānaṁ āyatanānaṁ evaṁ assādañca assādato, ādīnavañca ādīnavato, nissaraṇañca nissaraṇato yathābhūtaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ, athāhaṁ, bhikkhave, sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya ‘anuttaraṁ sammāsambodhiṁ abhisambuddho’ti paccaññāsiṁ.
sn35.14:2.3 Ñāṇañca pana me dassanaṁ udapādi:
sn35.14:2.4 ‘akuppā me vimutti, ayamantimā jāti, natthi dāni punabbhavo’”ti.

sn35.17:0.3 Paṭhamanoceassādasutta
sn35.17:1.1 “No cedaṁ, bhikkhave, cakkhussa assādo abhavissa, nayidaṁ sattā cakkhusmiṁ sārajjeyyuṁ.
sn35.17:1.2 Yasmā ca kho, bhikkhave, atthi cakkhussa assādo tasmā sattā cakkhusmiṁ sārajjanti.
sn35.17:1.3 No cedaṁ, bhikkhave, cakkhussa ādīnavo abhavissa, nayidaṁ sattā cakkhusmiṁ nibbindeyyuṁ.
sn35.17:1.4 Yasmā ca kho, bhikkhave, atthi cakkhussa ādīnavo tasmā sattā cakkhusmiṁ nibbindanti.
sn35.17:1.5 No cedaṁ, bhikkhave, cakkhussa nissaraṇaṁ abhavissa, nayidaṁ sattā cakkhusmā nissareyyuṁ.
sn35.17:1.6 Yasmā ca kho, bhikkhave, atthi cakkhussa nissaraṇaṁ tasmā sattā cakkhusmā nissaranti.
sn35.17:1.7 No cedaṁ, bhikkhave, sotassa assādo abhavissa …
sn35.17:1.8 no cedaṁ, bhikkhave, ghānassa assādo abhavissa …
sn35.17:1.9 no cedaṁ, bhikkhave, jivhāya assādo abhavissa, nayidaṁ sattā jivhāya sārajjeyyuṁ.
sn35.17:1.10 Yasmā ca kho, bhikkhave, atthi jivhāya assādo, tasmā sattā jivhāya sārajjanti.
sn35.17:1.11 No cedaṁ, bhikkhave, jivhāya ādīnavo abhavissa, nayidaṁ sattā jivhāya nibbindeyyuṁ.
sn35.17:1.12 Yasmā ca kho, bhikkhave, atthi jivhāya ādīnavo, tasmā sattā jivhāya nibbindanti.
sn35.17:1.13 No cedaṁ, bhikkhave, jivhāya nissaraṇaṁ abhavissa, nayidaṁ sattā jivhāya nissareyyuṁ.
sn35.17:1.14 Yasmā ca kho, bhikkhave, atthi jivhāya nissaraṇaṁ, tasmā sattā jivhāya nissaranti.
sn35.17:1.15 No cedaṁ, bhikkhave, kāyassa assādo abhavissa …
sn35.17:1.16 no cedaṁ, bhikkhave, manassa assādo abhavissa, nayidaṁ sattā manasmiṁ sārajjeyyuṁ.
sn35.17:1.17 Yasmā ca kho, bhikkhave, atthi manassa assādo, tasmā sattā manasmiṁ sārajjanti.
sn35.17:1.18 No cedaṁ, bhikkhave, manassa ādīnavo abhavissa, nayidaṁ sattā manasmiṁ nibbindeyyuṁ.
sn35.17:1.19 Yasmā ca kho, bhikkhave, atthi manassa ādīnavo, tasmā sattā manasmiṁ nibbindanti.
sn35.17:1.20 No cedaṁ, bhikkhave, manassa nissaraṇaṁ abhavissa, nayidaṁ sattā manasmā nissareyyuṁ.
sn35.17:1.21 Yasmā ca kho, bhikkhave, atthi manassa nissaraṇaṁ, tasmā sattā manasmā nissaranti.
sn35.17:2.1 Yāvakīvañca, bhikkhave, sattā imesaṁ channaṁ ajjhattikānaṁ āyatanānaṁ assādañca assādato, ādīnavañca ādīnavato, nissaraṇañca nissaraṇato yathābhūtaṁ nābbhaññaṁsu, neva tāva, bhikkhave, sattā sadevakā lokā samārakā sabrahmakā sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya nissaṭā visaññuttā vippamuttā vimariyādīkatena cetasā vihariṁsu.
sn35.17:2.2 Yato ca kho, bhikkhave, sattā imesaṁ channaṁ ajjhattikānaṁ āyatanānaṁ assādañca assādato, ādīnavañca ādīnavato, nissaraṇañca nissaraṇato yathābhūtaṁ abbhaññaṁsu, atha, bhikkhave, sattā sadevakā lokā samārakā sabrahmakā sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya nissaṭā visaññuttā vippamuttā vimariyādīkatena cetasā viharantī”ti.

sn35.22:3.2 Assādena apare duve;

sn35.22:3.4 Abhinandena apare duve;
sn35.22:3.5 Uppādena duve vuttā,
sn35.22:3.6 Vaggo tena pavuccatīti. "

sn35.23:1.4 Kiñca, bhikkhave, sabbaṁ?
sn35.23:1.5 Cakkhuñceva rūpā ca, sotañca saddā ca, ghānañca gandhā ca, jivhā ca rasā ca, kāyo ca phoṭṭhabbā ca, mano ca dhammā ca—
sn35.23:1.6 idaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, sabbaṁ.
sn35.23:1.7 Yo, bhikkhave, evaṁ vadeyya:
sn35.23:1.8 ‘ahametaṁ sabbaṁ paccakkhāya aññaṁ sabbaṁ paññāpessāmī’ti, tassa vācāvatthukamevassa;

sn35.23:1.11 Yathā taṁ, bhikkhave, avisayasmin”ti.

sn35.27:0.3 Dutiyaaparijānanasutta
sn35.27:1.1 “Sabbaṁ, bhikkhave, anabhijānaṁ aparijānaṁ avirājayaṁ appajahaṁ abhabbo dukkhakkhayāya.

sn35.27:1.3 Yañca, bhikkhave, cakkhu, ye ca rūpā, yañca cakkhuviññāṇaṁ, ye ca cakkhuviññāṇaviññātabbā dhammā …pe…
sn35.27:1.4 yā ca jivhā, ye ca rasā, yañca jivhāviññāṇaṁ, ye ca jivhāviññāṇaviññātabbā dhammā;
sn35.27:1.5 yo ca kāyo, ye ca phoṭṭhabbā, yañca kāyaviññāṇaṁ, ye ca kāyaviññāṇaviññātabbā dhammā;
sn35.27:1.6 yo ca mano, ye ca dhammā, yañca manoviññāṇaṁ, ye ca manoviññāṇaviññātabbā dhammā—
sn35.27:1.7 idaṁ kho, bhikkhave, sabbaṁ anabhijānaṁ aparijānaṁ avirājayaṁ appajahaṁ abhabbo dukkhakkhayāya.

sn35.27:2.2 Kiñca, bhikkhave, sabbaṁ abhijānaṁ parijānaṁ virājayaṁ pajahaṁ bhabbo dukkhakkhayāya?

sn35.27:2.4 yā ca jivhā, ye ca rasā, yañca jivhāviññāṇaṁ, ye ca jivhāviññāṇaviññātabbā dhammā;
sn35.27:2.5 yo ca kāyo, ye ca phoṭṭhabbā, yañca kāyaviññāṇaṁ, ye ca kāyaviññāṇaviññātabbā dhammā;
sn35.27:2.6 yo ca mano, ye ca dhammā, yañca manoviññāṇaṁ, ye ca manoviññāṇaviññātabbā dhammā—

sn35.28:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.28
sn35.28:0.2 3. Sabbavagga
sn35.28:0.3 Ādittasutta
sn35.28:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā gayāyaṁ viharati gayāsīse saddhiṁ bhikkhusahassena.
sn35.28:1.2 Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi:
sn35.28:1.3 “sabbaṁ, bhikkhave, ādittaṁ.
sn35.28:1.4 Kiñca, bhikkhave, sabbaṁ ādittaṁ?
sn35.28:1.5 Cakkhu, bhikkhave, ādittaṁ, rūpā ādittā, cakkhuviññāṇaṁ ādittaṁ, cakkhusamphasso āditto. Yampidaṁ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi ādittaṁ.
sn35.28:1.6 Kena ādittaṁ?
sn35.28:1.7 ‘Rāgagginā, dosagginā, mohagginā ādittaṁ, jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi ādittan’ti vadāmi …pe…
sn35.28:1.8 jivhā ādittā, rasā ādittā, jivhāviññāṇaṁ ādittaṁ, jivhāsamphasso āditto. Yampidaṁ jivhāsamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi ādittaṁ.
sn35.28:1.9 Kena ādittaṁ?
sn35.28:1.10 ‘Rāgagginā, dosagginā, mohagginā ādittaṁ, jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi ādittan’ti vadāmi …pe…
sn35.28:1.11 mano āditto, dhammā ādittā, manoviññāṇaṁ ādittaṁ, manosamphasso āditto. Yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi ādittaṁ.
sn35.28:1.12 Kena ādittaṁ?
sn35.28:1.13 ‘Rāgagginā, dosagginā, mohagginā ādittaṁ, jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi ādittan’ti vadāmi.
sn35.28:1.14 Evaṁ passaṁ, bhikkhave, sutavā ariyasāvako cakkhusmimpi nibbindati, rūpesupi nibbindati, cakkhuviññāṇepi nibbindati, cakkhusamphassepi nibbindati, yampidaṁ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tasmimpi nibbindati …pe…
sn35.28:1.15 yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tasmimpi nibbindati.
sn35.28:1.16 Nibbindaṁ virajjati; virāgā vimuccati; vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti.
sn35.28:1.17 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.
sn35.28:2.1 Idamavoca bhagavā.
sn35.28:2.2 Attamanā te bhikkhū bhagavato bhāsitaṁ abhinanduṁ.
sn35.28:2.3 Imasmiñca pana veyyākaraṇasmiṁ bhaññamāne tassa bhikkhusahassassa anupādāya āsavehi cittāni vimucciṁsūti.

sn35.29:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.29
sn35.29:0.2 3. Sabbavagga
sn35.29:0.3 Addhabhūtasutta
sn35.29:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ—
sn35.29:1.2 ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe.
sn35.29:1.3 Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi:
sn35.29:1.4 “sabbaṁ, bhikkhave, addhabhūtaṁ.
sn35.29:1.5 Kiñca, bhikkhave, sabbaṁ addhabhūtaṁ?
sn35.29:1.6 Cakkhu, bhikkhave, addhabhūtaṁ, rūpā addhabhūtā, cakkhuviññāṇaṁ addhabhūtaṁ, cakkhusamphasso addhabhūto, yampidaṁ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi addhabhūtaṁ.
sn35.29:1.7 Kena addhabhūtaṁ?
sn35.29:1.8 ‘Jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi addhabhūtan’ti vadāmi …pe…
sn35.29:1.9 jivhā addhabhūtā, rasā addhabhūtā, jivhāviññāṇaṁ addhabhūtaṁ, jivhāsamphasso addhabhūto, yampidaṁ jivhāsamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi addhabhūtaṁ.
sn35.29:1.10 Kena addhabhūtaṁ?
sn35.29:1.11 ‘Jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi addhabhūtan’ti vadāmi.
sn35.29:1.12 Kāyo addhabhūto …pe…
sn35.29:1.13 mano addhabhūto, dhammā addhabhūtā, manoviññāṇaṁ addhabhūtaṁ, manosamphasso addhabhūto, yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi addhabhūtaṁ.
sn35.29:1.14 Kena addhabhūtaṁ?
sn35.29:1.15 ‘Jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi addhabhūtan’ti vadāmi.
sn35.29:1.16 Evaṁ passaṁ, bhikkhave, sutavā ariyasāvako cakkhusmimpi nibbindati, rūpesupi nibbindati, cakkhuviññāṇepi nibbindati, cakkhusamphassepi nibbindati …pe…
sn35.29:1.17 yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tasmimpi nibbindati.
sn35.29:1.18 Nibbindaṁ virajjati, virāgā vimuccati, vimuttasmiṁ ‘vimuttam’iti ñāṇaṁ hoti,
sn35.29:1.19 ‘khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.
sn35.29:1.20 Sattamaṁ. "
sn35.30:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.30
sn35.30:0.2 3. Sabbavagga
sn35.30:0.3 Samugghātasāruppasutta
sn35.30:1.1 “Sabbamaññitasamugghātasāruppaṁ vo, bhikkhave, paṭipadaṁ desessāmi.
sn35.30:1.2 Taṁ suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmīti.
sn35.30:1.3 Katamā ca sā, bhikkhave, sabbamaññitasamugghātasāruppā paṭipadā?
sn35.30:1.4 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu cakkhuṁ na maññati, cakkhusmiṁ na maññati, cakkhuto na maññati, cakkhuṁ meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.5 Rūpe na maññati, rūpesu na maññati, rūpato na maññati, rūpā meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.6 Cakkhuviññāṇaṁ na maññati, cakkhuviññāṇasmiṁ na maññati, cakkhuviññāṇato na maññati, cakkhuviññāṇaṁ meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.7 Cakkhusamphassaṁ na maññati, cakkhusamphassasmiṁ na maññati, cakkhusamphassato na maññati, cakkhusamphasso meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.8 Yampidaṁ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi na maññati, tasmimpi na maññati, tatopi na maññati, taṁ meti na maññati …pe…
sn35.30:1.9 jivhaṁ na maññati, jivhāya na maññati, jivhāto na maññati, jivhā meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.10 Rase na maññati, rasesu na maññati, rasato na maññati, rasā meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.11 Jivhāviññāṇaṁ na maññati, jivhāviññāṇasmiṁ na maññati, jivhāviññāṇato na maññati, jivhāviññāṇaṁ meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.12 Jivhāsamphassaṁ na maññati, jivhāsamphassasmiṁ na maññati, jivhāsamphassato na maññati, jivhāsamphasso meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.13 Yampidaṁ jivhāsamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi na maññati, tasmimpi na maññati, tatopi na maññati, taṁ meti na maññati …pe…
sn35.30:1.14 manaṁ na maññati, manasmiṁ na maññati, manato na maññati, mano meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.15 Dhamme na maññati, dhammesu na maññati, dhammato na maññati, dhammā meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.16 Manoviññāṇaṁ na maññati, manoviññāṇasmiṁ na maññati, manoviññāṇato na maññati, manoviññāṇaṁ meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.17 Manosamphassaṁ na maññati, manosamphassasmiṁ na maññati, manosamphassato na maññati, manosamphasso meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.18 Yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi na maññati, tasmimpi na maññati, tatopi na maññati, taṁ meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.19 Sabbaṁ na maññati, sabbasmiṁ na maññati, sabbato na maññati, sabbaṁ meti na maññati.
sn35.30:1.20 So evaṁ amaññamāno na ca kiñci loke upādiyati.
sn35.30:1.21 Anupādiyaṁ na paritassati. Aparitassaṁ paccattaññeva parinibbāyati.
sn35.30:1.22 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānāti.
sn35.30:1.23 Ayaṁ kho sā, bhikkhave, sabbamaññitasamugghātasāruppā paṭipadā”ti.

sn35.64:2.3 Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato uppajjati nandī.
sn35.64:2.4 Nandisamudayā dukkhasamudayo, migajālāti vadāmi …pe…
sn35.64:2.5 santi ca kho, migajāla, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe…
sn35.64:2.6 santi ca kho, migajāla, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.64:2.7 Tañce bhikkhu abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.64:2.8 Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato uppajjati nandī.
sn35.64:2.9 Nandisamudayā dukkhasamudayo, migajālāti vadāmi.
sn35.64:3.1 Santi ca kho, migajāla, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.64:3.2 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati. Tassa taṁ anabhinandato anabhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato nandī nirujjhati.
sn35.64:3.3 Nandinirodhā dukkhanirodho, migajālāti vadāmi …pe…
sn35.64:3.4 santi ca kho, migajāla, jivhāviññeyyā rasā iṭṭhā kantā …pe…
sn35.64:3.5 santi ca kho, migajāla, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.64:3.6 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati. Tassa taṁ anabhinandato anabhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato nandī nirujjhati.
sn35.64:3.7 Nandinirodhā dukkhanirodho, migajālāti vadāmī”ti.
sn35.64:4.1 Atha kho āyasmā migajālo bhagavato bhāsitaṁ abhinanditvā anumoditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṁ katvā pakkāmi.
sn35.64:4.2 Atha kho āyasmā migajālo eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharato nacirasseva—yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaṁ pabbajanti, tadanuttaraṁ—brahmacariyapariyosānaṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi.
sn35.64:4.3 “Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā”ti abbhaññāsi.
sn35.64:4.4 Aññataro ca panāyasmā migajālo arahataṁ ahosīti.
sn35.64:4.5 Dutiyaṁ. "

sn35.69:2.13 ‘ahaṁ cakkhūti vā mama cakkhūti vā …pe…
sn35.69:2.14 ahaṁ jivhāti vā mama jivhāti vā …pe…

sn35.69:2.16 Tassa mayhañca kho, āvuso sāriputta, kiṁ kāyassa vā aññathattaṁ bhavissati, indriyānaṁ vā vipariṇāmo”ti.

sn35.73:1.1 “Yo hi koci, bhikkhave, bhikkhu channaṁ phassāyatanānaṁ samudayañca atthaṅgamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti.
sn35.73:1.2 Avusitaṁ tena brahmacariyaṁ, ārakā so imasmā dhammavinayā”ti.
sn35.73:2.1 Evaṁ vutte, aññataro bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.73:2.2 “etthāhaṁ, bhante, anassasaṁ panassasaṁ.
sn35.73:2.3 Ahañhi, bhante, channaṁ phassāyatanānaṁ samudayañca atthaṅgamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāmī”ti.
sn35.73:3.1 “Taṁ kiṁ maññasi, bhikkhu,
sn35.73:3.2 cakkhu niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.73:4.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.73:5.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vā taṁ sukhaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.73:6.1 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.73:7.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ:
sn35.73:7.2 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’”ti?
sn35.73:8.1 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.73:9.1 “Sotaṁ …
sn35.73:9.2 ghānaṁ …
sn35.73:9.3 jivhā …
sn35.73:9.4 kāyo …
sn35.73:9.5 mano nicco vā anicco vā”ti?
sn35.73:10.1 “Anicco, bhante”.
sn35.73:11.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vā taṁ sukhaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.73:12.1 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.73:13.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ:
sn35.73:13.2 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’”ti?
sn35.73:14.1 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.73:15.1 “Evaṁ passaṁ, bhikkhu, sutavā ariyasāvako cakkhusmimpi nibbindati, sotasmimpi nibbindati, ghānasmimpi nibbindati, jivhāyapi nibbindati, kāyasmimpi nibbindati, manasmimpi nibbindati.
sn35.73:15.2 Nibbindaṁ virajjati; virāgā vimuccati; vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti.
sn35.73:15.3 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.
sn35.73:15.4 Ekādasamaṁ.
sn35.73:15.5 Migajālavaggo dutiyo.
sn35.73:16.0 Tassuddānaṁ
sn35.73:16.1 Migajālena dve vuttā,
sn35.73:16.2 Cattāro ca samiddhinā;
sn35.73:16.3 Upaseno upavāṇo,
sn35.73:16.4 Chaphassāyatanikā tayoti. "
sn35.74:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.74
sn35.74:0.2 8. Gilānavagga
sn35.74:0.3 Paṭhamagilānasutta
sn35.74:1.1 Sāvatthinidānaṁ.
sn35.74:1.2 Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami …pe… ekamantaṁ nisinno kho so bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.74:1.3 “amukasmiṁ, bhante, vihāre aññataro bhikkhu navo appaññāto ābādhiko dukkhito bāḷhagilāno.
sn35.74:1.4 Sādhu, bhante, bhagavā yena so bhikkhu tenupasaṅkamatu anukampaṁ upādāyā”ti.
sn35.74:2.1 Atha kho bhagavā navavādañca sutvā gilānavādañca, “appaññāto bhikkhū”ti iti viditvā yena so bhikkhu tenupasaṅkami.
sn35.74:2.2 Addasā kho so bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ dūratova āgacchantaṁ.
sn35.74:2.3 Disvāna mañcake samadhosi.
sn35.74:2.4 Atha kho bhagavā taṁ bhikkhuṁ etadavoca:
sn35.74:2.5 “alaṁ, bhikkhu, mā tvaṁ mañcake samadhosi.
sn35.74:2.6 Santimāni āsanāni paññattāni, tatthāhaṁ nisīdissāmī”ti.
sn35.74:2.7 Nisīdi bhagavā paññatte āsane.
sn35.74:2.8 Nisajja kho bhagavā taṁ bhikkhuṁ etadavoca:
sn35.74:2.9 “kacci te, bhikkhu, khamanīyaṁ, kacci yāpanīyaṁ, kacci dukkhā vedanā paṭikkamanti no abhikkamanti, paṭikkamosānaṁ paññāyati no abhikkamo”ti?
sn35.74:3.1 “Na me, bhante, khamanīyaṁ, na yāpanīyaṁ, bāḷhā me dukkhā vedanā abhikkamanti no paṭikkamanti, abhikkamosānaṁ paññāyati no paṭikkamo”ti.
sn35.74:4.1 “Kacci te, bhikkhu, na kiñci kukkuccaṁ, na koci vippaṭisāro”ti?
sn35.74:5.1 “Taggha me, bhante, anappakaṁ kukkuccaṁ, anappako vippaṭisāro”ti.
sn35.74:6.1 “Kacci pana taṁ, bhikkhu, attā sīlato upavadatī”ti?
sn35.74:7.1 “Na kho maṁ, bhante, attā sīlato upavadatī”ti.
sn35.74:8.1 “No ce kira te, bhikkhu, attā sīlato upavadati, atha kiñca te kukkuccaṁ ko ca vippaṭisāro”ti?
sn35.74:9.1 “Na khvāhaṁ, bhante, sīlavisuddhatthaṁ bhagavatā dhammaṁ desitaṁ ājānāmī”ti.
sn35.74:10.1 “No ce kira tvaṁ, bhikkhu, sīlavisuddhatthaṁ mayā dhammaṁ desitaṁ ājānāsi, atha kimatthaṁ carahi tvaṁ, bhikkhu, mayā dhammaṁ desitaṁ ājānāsī”ti?
sn35.74:11.1 “Rāgavirāgatthaṁ khvāhaṁ, bhante, bhagavatā dhammaṁ desitaṁ ājānāmī”ti.
sn35.74:12.1 “Sādhu sādhu, bhikkhu.
sn35.74:12.2 Sādhu kho tvaṁ, bhikkhu, rāgavirāgatthaṁ mayā dhammaṁ desitaṁ ājānāsi.
sn35.74:12.3 Rāgavirāgattho hi, bhikkhu, mayā dhammo desito.
sn35.74:12.4 Taṁ kiṁ maññasi, bhikkhu,
sn35.74:12.5 cakkhu niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.74:13.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.74:14.1 “ …pe…
sn35.74:14.2 Sotaṁ …
sn35.74:14.3 ghānaṁ …
sn35.74:14.4 jivhā …
sn35.74:14.5 kāyo …
sn35.74:14.6 mano nicco vā anicco vā”ti?
sn35.74:15.1 “Anicco, bhante”.
sn35.74:16.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vā taṁ sukhaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.74:17.1 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.74:18.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ:
sn35.74:18.2 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’”ti?
sn35.74:19.1 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.74:20.1 “Evaṁ passaṁ, bhikkhu, sutavā ariyasāvako cakkhusmimpi nibbindati, sotasmimpi nibbindati …pe… manasmimpi nibbindati.
sn35.74:20.2 Nibbindaṁ virajjati; virāgā vimuccati; vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti.
sn35.74:20.3 ‘Khīṇā jāti …pe… nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.
sn35.74:21.1 Idamavoca bhagavā.
sn35.74:21.2 Attamano so bhikkhu bhagavato bhāsitaṁ abhinandi.
sn35.74:21.3 Imasmiñca pana veyyākaraṇasmiṁ bhaññamāne tassa bhikkhuno virajaṁ vītamalaṁ dhammacakkhuṁ udapādi:
sn35.74:21.4 “yaṁ kiñci samudayadhammaṁ sabbaṁ taṁ nirodhadhamman”ti.
sn35.74:21.5 Paṭhamaṁ. "

sn35.87:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.87
sn35.87:0.2 9. Channavagga
sn35.87:0.3 Channasutta
sn35.87:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe.
sn35.87:1.2 Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā ca sāriputto āyasmā ca mahācundo āyasmā ca channo gijjhakūṭe pabbate viharanti.
sn35.87:1.3 Tena kho pana samayena yena āyasmā channo ābādhiko hoti dukkhito bāḷhagilāno.
sn35.87:1.4 Atha kho āyasmā sāriputto sāyanhasamayaṁ paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā mahācundo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ mahācundaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.87:1.5 “āyāmāvuso cunda, yenāyasmā channo tenupasaṅkamissāma gilānapucchakā”ti.
sn35.87:1.6 “Evamāvuso”ti kho āyasmā mahācundo āyasmato sāriputtassa paccassosi.
sn35.87:2.1 Atha kho āyasmā ca sāriputto āyasmā ca mahācundo yenāyasmā channo tenupasaṅkamiṁsu; upasaṅkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdiṁsu. Nisajja kho āyasmā sāriputto āyasmantaṁ channaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.87:2.2 “kacci te, āvuso channa, khamanīyaṁ, kacci yāpanīyaṁ, kacci dukkhā vedanā paṭikkamanti no abhikkamanti, paṭikkamosānaṁ paññāyati no abhikkamo”ti?
sn35.87:3.1 “Na me, āvuso sāriputta, khamanīyaṁ na yāpanīyaṁ, bāḷhā me dukkhā vedanā abhikkamanti no paṭikkamanti, abhikkamosānaṁ paññāyati no paṭikkamo.
sn35.87:3.2 Seyyathāpi, āvuso, balavā puriso tiṇhena sikharena muddhani abhimattheyya; evameva kho, āvuso, adhimattā vātā muddhani ūhananti.
sn35.87:3.3 Na me, āvuso, khamanīyaṁ, na yāpanīyaṁ …pe… no paṭikkamo.
sn35.87:3.4 Seyyathāpi, āvuso, balavā puriso daḷhena varattakkhaṇḍena sīse sīsaveṭhaṁ dadeyya; evameva kho, āvuso, adhimattā sīse sīsavedanā.
sn35.87:3.5 Na me, āvuso, khamanīyaṁ, na yāpanīyaṁ …pe… no paṭikkamo.
sn35.87:3.6 Seyyathāpi, āvuso, dakkho goghātako vā goghātakantevāsī vā tiṇhena govikantanena kucchiṁ parikanteyya; evameva kho adhimattā vātā kucchiṁ parikantanti.
sn35.87:3.7 Na me, āvuso, khamanīyaṁ, na yāpanīyaṁ …pe… no paṭikkamo.
sn35.87:3.8 Seyyathāpi, āvuso, dve balavanto purisā dubbalataraṁ purisaṁ nānābāhāsu gahetvā aṅgārakāsuyā santāpeyyuṁ samparitāpeyyuṁ; evameva kho, āvuso, adhimatto kāyasmiṁ ḍāho.
sn35.87:3.9 Na me, āvuso, khamanīyaṁ, na yāpanīyaṁ, bāḷhā me dukkhā vedanā abhikkamanti no paṭikkamanti, abhikkamosānaṁ paññāyati no paṭikkamo.
sn35.87:3.10 Satthaṁ, āvuso sāriputta, āharissāmi, nāvakaṅkhāmi jīvitan”ti.
sn35.87:4.1 “Mā āyasmā channo satthaṁ āharesi.
sn35.87:4.2 Yāpetāyasmā channo, yāpentaṁ mayaṁ āyasmantaṁ channaṁ icchāma.
sn35.87:4.3 Sace āyasmato channassa natthi sappāyāni bhojanāni, ahaṁ āyasmato channassa sappāyāni bhojanāni pariyesissāmi.
sn35.87:4.4 Sace āyasmato channassa natthi sappāyāni bhesajjāni, ahaṁ āyasmato channassa sappāyāni bhesajjāni pariyesissāmi.
sn35.87:4.5 Sace āyasmato channassa natthi patirūpā upaṭṭhākā, ahaṁ āyasmantaṁ channaṁ upaṭṭhahissāmi.
sn35.87:4.6 Mā āyasmā channo satthaṁ āharesi.
sn35.87:4.7 Yāpetāyasmā channo, yāpentaṁ mayaṁ āyasmantaṁ channaṁ icchāmā”ti.
sn35.87:5.1 “Na me, āvuso sāriputta, natthi sappāyāni bhojanāni;
sn35.87:5.2 atthi me sappāyāni bhojanāni.
sn35.87:5.3 Napi me natthi sappāyāni bhesajjāni;
sn35.87:5.4 atthi me sappāyāni bhesajjāni.
sn35.87:5.5 Napi me natthi patirūpā upaṭṭhākā;
sn35.87:5.6 atthi me patirūpā upaṭṭhākā.
sn35.87:5.7 Api ca me, āvuso, satthā pariciṇṇo dīgharattaṁ manāpeneva, no amanāpena.
sn35.87:5.8 Etañhi, āvuso, sāvakassa patirūpaṁ yaṁ satthāraṁ paricareyya manāpeneva, no amanāpena.
sn35.87:5.9 ‘Anupavajjaṁ channo bhikkhu satthaṁ āharissatī’ti—evametaṁ, āvuso sāriputta, dhārehī”ti.
sn35.87:6.1 “Puccheyyāma mayaṁ āyasmantaṁ channaṁ kañcideva desaṁ, sace āyasmā channo okāsaṁ karoti pañhassa veyyākaraṇāyā”ti.
sn35.87:6.2 “Pucchāvuso sāriputta, sutvā vedissāmā”ti.
sn35.87:7.1 “Cakkhuṁ, āvuso channa, cakkhuviññāṇaṁ cakkhuviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’ti samanupassasi …pe…
sn35.87:7.2 jivhaṁ, āvuso channa, jivhāviññāṇaṁ jivhāviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’ti samanupassasi …pe…
sn35.87:7.3 manaṁ, āvuso channa, manoviññāṇaṁ manoviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’ti samanupassasī”ti?
sn35.87:8.1 “Cakkhuṁ, āvuso sāriputta, cakkhuviññāṇaṁ cakkhuviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti samanupassāmi …pe…
sn35.87:8.2 jivhaṁ, āvuso sāriputta, jivhāviññāṇaṁ jivhāviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti samanupassāmi …pe…
sn35.87:8.3 manaṁ, āvuso sāriputta, manoviññāṇaṁ manoviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti samanupassāmī”ti.
sn35.87:9.1 “Cakkhusmiṁ, āvuso channa, cakkhuviññāṇe cakkhuviññāṇaviññātabbesu dhammesu kiṁ disvā kiṁ abhiññāya cakkhuṁ cakkhuviññāṇaṁ cakkhuviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti samanupassasi …
sn35.87:9.2 jivhāya, āvuso channa, jivhāviññāṇe jivhāviññāṇaviññātabbesu dhammesu kiṁ disvā kiṁ abhiññāya jivhaṁ jivhāviññāṇaṁ jivhāviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti samanupassasi …
sn35.87:9.3 manasmiṁ, āvuso channa, manoviññāṇe manoviññāṇaviññātabbesu dhammesu kiṁ disvā kiṁ abhiññāya manaṁ manoviññāṇaṁ manoviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti samanupassasī”ti?
sn35.87:10.1 “Cakkhusmiṁ, āvuso sāriputta, cakkhuviññāṇe cakkhuviññāṇaviññātabbesu dhammesu nirodhaṁ disvā nirodhaṁ abhiññāya cakkhuṁ cakkhuviññāṇaṁ cakkhuviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti samanupassāmi …pe…
sn35.87:10.2 jivhāya, āvuso sāriputta, jivhāviññāṇe jivhāviññāṇaviññātabbesu dhammesu nirodhaṁ disvā nirodhaṁ abhiññāya jivhaṁ jivhāviññāṇaṁ jivhāviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti samanupassāmi …pe…
sn35.87:10.3 manasmiṁ, āvuso sāriputta, manoviññāṇe manoviññāṇaviññātabbesu dhammesu nirodhaṁ disvā nirodhaṁ abhiññāya manaṁ manoviññāṇaṁ manoviññāṇaviññātabbe dhamme ‘netaṁ mama, nesohamasmi, na meso attā’ti samanupassāmī”ti.
sn35.87:11.1 Evaṁ vutte, āyasmā mahācundo āyasmantaṁ channaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.87:11.2 “tasmātiha, āvuso channa, idampi tassa bhagavato sāsanaṁ niccakappaṁ sādhukaṁ manasi kātabbaṁ:
sn35.87:11.3 ‘nissitassa calitaṁ, anissitassa calitaṁ natthi.
sn35.87:11.4 Calite asati passaddhi hoti.
sn35.87:11.5 Passaddhiyā sati nati na hoti.
sn35.87:11.6 Natiyā asati āgatigati na hoti.
sn35.87:11.7 Āgatigatiyā asati cutūpapāto na hoti.
sn35.87:11.8 Cutūpapāte asati nevidha na huraṁ na ubhayamantarena.
sn35.87:11.9 Esevanto dukkhassā’”ti.
sn35.87:12.1 Atha kho āyasmā ca sāriputto āyasmā ca mahācundo āyasmantaṁ channaṁ iminā ovādena ovaditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkamiṁsu.
sn35.87:12.2 Atha kho āyasmā channo acirapakkantesu tesu āyasmantesu satthaṁ āharesi.
sn35.87:13.1 Atha kho āyasmā sāriputto yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā sāriputto bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.87:13.2 “āyasmatā, bhante, channena satthaṁ āharitaṁ.
sn35.87:13.3 Tassa kā gati ko abhisamparāyo”ti?
sn35.87:13.4 “Nanu te, sāriputta, channena bhikkhunā sammukhāyeva anupavajjatā byākatā”ti?
sn35.87:13.5 “Atthi, bhante, pubbavijjanaṁ nāma vajjigāmo.
sn35.87:13.6 Tatthāyasmato channassa mittakulāni suhajjakulāni upavajjakulānī”ti.
sn35.87:13.7 “Honti hete, sāriputta, channassa bhikkhuno mittakulāni suhajjakulāni upavajjakulāni.
sn35.87:13.8 Na kho panāhaṁ, sāriputta, ettāvatā saupavajjoti vadāmi.
sn35.87:13.9 Yo kho, sāriputta, tañca kāyaṁ nikkhipati, aññañca kāyaṁ upādiyati, tamahaṁ saupavajjoti vadāmi.
sn35.87:13.10 Taṁ channassa bhikkhuno natthi.
sn35.87:13.11 ‘Anupavajjaṁ channena bhikkhunā satthaṁ āharitan’ti—
sn35.87:13.12 evametaṁ, sāriputta, dhārehī”ti.
sn35.87:13.13 Catutthaṁ. "
sn35.88:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.88
sn35.88:0.2 9. Channavagga
sn35.88:0.3 Puṇṇasutta
sn35.88:1.1 Atha kho āyasmā puṇṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā …pe… ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā puṇṇo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.88:1.2 “sādhu me, bhante, bhagavā saṅkhittena dhammaṁ desetu, yamahaṁ bhagavato dhammaṁ sutvā eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto vihareyyan”ti.
sn35.88:2.1 “Santi kho, puṇṇa, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.88:2.2 Tañce bhikkhu abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.88:2.3 Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato uppajjati nandī.
sn35.88:2.4 ‘Nandisamudayā dukkhasamudayo, puṇṇā’ti vadāmi …pe…
sn35.88:2.5 santi kho, puṇṇa, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe…
sn35.88:2.6 santi kho, puṇṇa, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.88:2.7 Tañce bhikkhu abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.88:2.8 Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato uppajjati nandī.
sn35.88:2.9 ‘Nandisamudayā dukkhasamudayo, puṇṇā’ti vadāmi.
sn35.88:3.1 Santi kho, puṇṇa, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.88:3.2 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati, tassa taṁ anabhinandato anabhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato nirujjhati nandī.
sn35.88:3.3 ‘Nandinirodhā dukkhanirodho, puṇṇā’ti vadāmi …pe…
sn35.88:3.4 santi kho, puṇṇa, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.88:3.5 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati, tassa taṁ anabhinandato anabhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato nirujjhati nandī.
sn35.88:3.6 ‘Nandinirodhā dukkhanirodho, puṇṇā’ti vadāmi.
sn35.88:4.1 Iminā tvaṁ, puṇṇa, mayā saṅkhittena ovādena ovadito katamasmiṁ janapade viharissasī”ti?
sn35.88:4.2 “Atthi, bhante, sunāparanto nāma janapado, tatthāhaṁ viharissāmī”ti.
sn35.88:5.1 “Caṇḍā kho, puṇṇa, sunāparantakā manussā;
sn35.88:5.2 pharusā kho, puṇṇa, sunāparantakā manussā.
sn35.88:5.3 Sace taṁ, puṇṇa, sunāparantakā manussā akkosissanti paribhāsissanti, tatra te, puṇṇa, kinti bhavissatī”ti?
sn35.88:6.1 “Sace maṁ, bhante, sunāparantakā manussā akkosissanti paribhāsissanti, tatra me evaṁ bhavissati:
sn35.88:6.2 ‘bhaddakā vatime sunāparantakā manussā, subhaddakā vatime sunāparantakā manussā, yaṁ me nayime pāṇinā pahāraṁ dentī’ti.
sn35.88:6.3 Evamettha, bhagavā, bhavissati;
sn35.88:6.4 evamettha, sugata, bhavissatī”ti.
sn35.88:7.1 “Sace pana te, puṇṇa, sunāparantakā manussā pāṇinā pahāraṁ dassanti, tatra pana te, puṇṇa, kinti bhavissatī”ti?
sn35.88:8.1 “Sace me, bhante, sunāparantakā manussā pāṇinā pahāraṁ dassanti, tatra me evaṁ bhavissati:
sn35.88:8.2 ‘bhaddakā vatime sunāparantakā manussā, subhaddakā vatime sunāparantakā manussā, yaṁ me nayime leḍḍunā pahāraṁ dentī’ti.
sn35.88:8.3 Evamettha, bhagavā, bhavissati;
sn35.88:8.4 evamettha, sugata, bhavissatī”ti.
sn35.88:9.1 “Sace pana te, puṇṇa, sunāparantakā manussā leḍḍunā pahāraṁ dassanti, tatra pana te, puṇṇa, kinti bhavissatī”ti?
sn35.88:10.1 “Sace me, bhante, sunāparantakā manussā leḍḍunā pahāraṁ dassanti, tatra me evaṁ bhavissati:
sn35.88:10.2 ‘bhaddakā vatime sunāparantakā manussā, subhaddakā vatime sunāparantakā manussā, yaṁ me nayime daṇḍena pahāraṁ dentī’ti.
sn35.88:10.3 Evamettha, bhagavā, bhavissati;
sn35.88:10.4 evamettha, sugata, bhavissatī”ti.
sn35.88:11.1 “Sace pana puṇṇa, sunāparantakā manussā daṇḍena pahāraṁ dassanti, tatra pana te, puṇṇa, kinti bhavissatī”ti?
sn35.88:12.1 “Sace me, bhante, sunāparantakā manussā daṇḍena pahāraṁ dassanti, tatra me evaṁ bhavissati:
sn35.88:12.2 ‘bhaddakā vatime sunāparantakā manussā, subhaddakā vatime sunāparantakā manussā, yaṁ me nayime satthena pahāraṁ dentī’ti.
sn35.88:12.3 Evamettha, bhagavā, bhavissati;
sn35.88:12.4 evamettha, sugata, bhavissatī”ti.
sn35.88:13.1 “Sace pana te, puṇṇa, sunāparantakā manussā satthena pahāraṁ dassanti, tatra pana te, puṇṇa, kinti bhavissatī”ti?
sn35.88:14.1 “Sace me, bhante, sunāparantakā manussā satthena pahāraṁ dassanti, tatra me evaṁ bhavissati:
sn35.88:14.2 ‘bhaddakā vatime sunāparantakā manussā, subhaddakā vatime sunāparantakā manussā, yaṁ maṁ nayime tiṇhena satthena jīvitā voropentī’ti.
sn35.88:14.3 Evamettha, bhagavā, bhavissati;
sn35.88:14.4 evamettha, sugata, bhavissatī”ti.
sn35.88:15.1 “Sace pana taṁ, puṇṇa, sunāparantakā manussā tiṇhena satthena jīvitā voropessanti, tatra pana te, puṇṇa, kinti bhavissatī”ti?
sn35.88:16.1 “Sace maṁ, bhante, sunāparantakā manussā tiṇhena satthena jīvitā voropessanti, tatra me evaṁ bhavissati:
sn35.88:16.2 ‘santi kho tassa bhagavato sāvakā kāyena ca jīvitena ca aṭṭīyamānā harāyamānā jigucchamānā satthahārakaṁ pariyesanti, taṁ me idaṁ apariyiṭṭhaññeva satthahārakaṁ laddhan’ti.
sn35.88:16.3 Evamettha, bhagavā, bhavissati;
sn35.88:16.4 evamettha, sugata, bhavissatī”ti.
sn35.88:17.1 “Sādhu sādhu, puṇṇa.
sn35.88:17.2 Sakkhissasi kho tvaṁ, puṇṇa, iminā damūpasamena samannāgato sunāparantasmiṁ janapade vatthuṁ.
sn35.88:17.3 Yassadāni tvaṁ, puṇṇa, kālaṁ maññasī”ti.
sn35.88:18.1 Atha kho āyasmā puṇṇo bhagavato vacanaṁ abhinanditvā anumoditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṁ katvā senāsanaṁ saṁsāmetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena sunāparanto janapado tena cārikaṁ pakkāmi.
sn35.88:18.2 Anupubbena cārikaṁ caramāno yena sunāparanto janapado tadavasari.
sn35.88:18.3 Tatra sudaṁ āyasmā puṇṇo sunāparantasmiṁ janapade viharati.
sn35.88:18.4 Atha kho āyasmā puṇṇo tenevantaravassena pañcamattāni upāsakasatāni paṭivedesi.
sn35.88:18.5 Tenevantaravassena pañcamattāni upāsikāsatāni paṭivedesi.
sn35.88:18.6 Tenevantaravassena tisso vijjā sacchākāsi.
sn35.88:18.7 Tenevantaravassena parinibbāyi.
sn35.88:19.1 Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṁsu …pe… ekamantaṁ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū bhagavantaṁ etadavocuṁ:
sn35.88:19.2 “yo so, bhante, puṇṇo nāma kulaputto bhagavatā saṅkhittena ovādena ovadito, so kālaṅkato.
sn35.88:19.3 Tassa kā gati ko abhisamparāyo”ti?
sn35.88:20.1 “Paṇḍito, bhikkhave, puṇṇo kulaputto, paccapādi dhammassānudhammaṁ, na ca maṁ dhammādhikaraṇaṁ vihesesi.
sn35.88:20.2 Parinibbuto, bhikkhave, puṇṇo kulaputto”ti.
sn35.88:20.3 Pañcamaṁ. "
sn35.89:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.89
sn35.89:0.2 9. Channavagga
sn35.89:0.3 Bāhiyasutta
sn35.89:1.1 Atha kho āyasmā bāhiyo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami …pe… ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā bāhiyo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.89:1.2 “sādhu me, bhante, bhagavā saṅkhittena dhammaṁ desetu, yamahaṁ bhagavato dhammaṁ sutvā eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto vihareyyan”ti.
sn35.89:2.1 “Taṁ kiṁ maññasi, bāhiya,
sn35.89:2.2 cakkhu niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.89:3.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.89:4.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vā taṁ sukhaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.89:5.1 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.89:6.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ:
sn35.89:6.2 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’”ti?
sn35.89:7.1 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.89:8.1 “Rūpā niccā vā aniccā vā”ti?
sn35.89:9.1 “Aniccā, bhante” …pe…
sn35.89:9.2 cakkhuviññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn35.89:9.3 cakkhusamphasso …pe…
sn35.89:9.4 yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.89:10.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.89:11.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vā taṁ sukhaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.89:12.1 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.89:13.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ:
sn35.89:13.2 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’”ti?
sn35.89:14.1 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.89:15.1 “Evaṁ passaṁ, bāhiya, sutavā ariyasāvako cakkhusmimpi nibbindati, rūpesupi nibbindati, cakkhuviññāṇepi nibbindati, cakkhusamphassepi nibbindati …pe…
sn35.89:15.2 yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tasmimpi nibbindati.
sn35.89:15.3 Nibbindaṁ virajjati; virāgā vimuccati; vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti.
sn35.89:15.4 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.
sn35.89:16.1 Atha kho āyasmā bāhiyo bhagavato bhāsitaṁ abhinanditvā anumoditvā uṭṭhāyāsanā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṁ katvā pakkāmi.
sn35.89:16.2 Atha kho āyasmā bāhiyo eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto nacirasseva—yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaṁ pabbajanti, tadanuttaraṁ—brahmacariyapariyosānaṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi.
sn35.89:16.3 “Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā”ti abbhaññāsi.
sn35.89:16.4 Aññataro ca panāyasmā bāhiyo arahataṁ ahosīti.
sn35.89:16.5 Chaṭṭhaṁ. "
sn35.90:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.90
sn35.90:0.2 9. Channavagga
sn35.90:0.3 Paṭhamaejāsutta
sn35.90:1.1 “Ejā, bhikkhave, rogo, ejā gaṇḍo, ejā sallaṁ.
sn35.90:1.2 Tasmātiha, bhikkhave, tathāgato anejo viharati vītasallo.
sn35.90:1.3 Tasmātiha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu cepi ākaṅkheyya ‘anejo vihareyyaṁ vītasallo’ti,
sn35.90:1.4 cakkhuṁ na maññeyya, cakkhusmiṁ na maññeyya, cakkhuto na maññeyya, cakkhu meti na maññeyya;
sn35.90:1.5 rūpe na maññeyya, rūpesu na maññeyya, rūpato na maññeyya, rūpā meti na maññeyya;
sn35.90:1.6 cakkhuviññāṇaṁ na maññeyya, cakkhuviññāṇasmiṁ na maññeyya, cakkhuviññāṇato na maññeyya, cakkhuviññāṇaṁ meti na maññeyya;
sn35.90:1.7 cakkhusamphassaṁ na maññeyya, cakkhusamphassasmiṁ na maññeyya, cakkhusamphassato na maññeyya, cakkhusamphasso meti na maññeyya.
sn35.90:1.8 Yampidaṁ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi na maññeyya, tasmimpi na maññeyya, tatopi na maññeyya, taṁ meti na maññeyya.
sn35.90:2.1 Sotaṁ na maññeyya …pe…
sn35.90:2.2 ghānaṁ na maññeyya …pe…
sn35.90:2.3 jivhaṁ na maññeyya, jivhāya na maññeyya, jivhāto na maññeyya, jivhā meti na maññeyya;
sn35.90:2.4 rase na maññeyya …pe…
sn35.90:2.5 jivhāviññāṇaṁ na maññeyya …pe…
sn35.90:2.6 jivhāsamphassaṁ na maññeyya …pe…
sn35.90:2.7 yampidaṁ jivhāsamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi na maññeyya, tasmimpi na maññeyya, tatopi na maññeyya, taṁ meti na maññeyya.
sn35.90:3.1 Kāyaṁ na maññeyya …pe…
sn35.90:3.2 manaṁ na maññeyya, manasmiṁ na maññeyya, manato na maññeyya, mano meti na maññeyya;
sn35.90:3.3 dhamme na maññeyya …pe…
sn35.90:3.4 mano viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn35.90:3.5 manosamphassaṁ …pe…
sn35.90:3.6 yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi na maññeyya, tasmimpi na maññeyya, tatopi na maññeyya, taṁ meti na maññeyya;
sn35.90:3.7 sabbaṁ na maññeyya, sabbasmiṁ na maññeyya, sabbato na maññeyya, sabbaṁ meti na maññeyya.
sn35.90:4.1 So evaṁ amaññamāno na kiñcipi loke upādiyati.
sn35.90:4.2 Anupādiyaṁ na paritassati. Aparitassaṁ paccattaññeva parinibbāyati.
sn35.90:4.3 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.

sn35.95:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.95
sn35.95:0.2 10. Saḷavagga
sn35.95:0.3 Mālukyaputtasutta
sn35.95:1.1 Atha kho āyasmā mālukyaputto yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami …pe… ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā mālukyaputto bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.95:1.2 “sādhu me, bhante, bhagavā saṅkhittena dhammaṁ desetu, yamahaṁ bhagavato dhammaṁ sutvā eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto vihareyyan”ti.
sn35.95:2.1 “Ettha dāni, mālukyaputta, kiṁ dahare bhikkhū vakkhāma.
sn35.95:2.2 Yatra hi nāma tvaṁ, bhikkhu, jiṇṇo vuddho mahallako addhagato vayoanuppatto saṅkhittena ovādaṁ yācasī”ti.
sn35.95:3.1 “Kiñcāpāhaṁ, bhante, jiṇṇo vuddho mahallako addhagato vayoanuppatto.
sn35.95:3.2 Desetu me, bhante, bhagavā saṅkhittena dhammaṁ, desetu sugato saṅkhittena dhammaṁ, appeva nāmāhaṁ bhagavato bhāsitassa atthaṁ ājāneyyaṁ. Appeva nāmāhaṁ bhagavato bhāsitassa dāyādo assan”ti.
sn35.95:4.1 “Taṁ kiṁ maññasi, mālukyaputta,
sn35.95:4.2 ye te cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā adiṭṭhā adiṭṭhapubbā, na ca passasi, na ca te hoti passeyyanti? Atthi te tattha chando vā rāgo vā pemaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.95:4.3 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.95:5.1 “Ye te sotaviññeyyā saddā assutā assutapubbā, na ca suṇāsi, na ca te hoti suṇeyyanti? Atthi te tattha chando vā rāgo vā pemaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.95:5.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.95:6.1 “Ye te ghānaviññeyyā gandhā aghāyitā aghāyitapubbā, na ca ghāyasi, na ca te hoti ghāyeyyanti? Atthi te tattha chando vā rāgo vā pemaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.95:6.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.95:7.1 “Ye te jivhāviññeyyā rasā asāyitā asāyitapubbā, na ca sāyasi, na ca te hoti sāyeyyanti? Atthi te tattha chando vā rāgo vā pemaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.95:7.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.95:8.1 “Ye te kāyaviññeyyā phoṭṭhabbā asamphuṭṭhā asamphuṭṭhapubbā, na ca phusasi, na ca te hoti phuseyyanti? Atthi te tattha chando vā rāgo vā pemaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.95:8.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.95:9.1 “Ye te manoviññeyyā dhammā aviññātā aviññātapubbā, na ca vijānāsi, na ca te hoti vijāneyyanti? Atthi te tattha chando vā rāgo vā pemaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.95:9.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.95:10.1 “Ettha ca te, mālukyaputta, diṭṭhasutamutaviññātabbesu dhammesu diṭṭhe diṭṭhamattaṁ bhavissati, sute sutamattaṁ bhavissati, mute mutamattaṁ bhavissati, viññāte viññātamattaṁ bhavissati.
sn35.95:10.2 Yato kho te, mālukyaputta, diṭṭhasutamutaviññātabbesu dhammesu diṭṭhe diṭṭhamattaṁ bhavissati, sute sutamattaṁ bhavissati, mute mutamattaṁ bhavissati, viññāte viññātamattaṁ bhavissati;
sn35.95:10.3 tato tvaṁ, mālukyaputta, na tena.
sn35.95:10.4 Yato tvaṁ, mālukyaputta, na tena;
sn35.95:10.5 tato tvaṁ, mālukyaputta, na tattha.
sn35.95:10.6 Yato tvaṁ, mālukyaputta, na tattha;
sn35.95:10.7 tato tvaṁ, mālukyaputta, nevidha, na huraṁ, na ubhayamantarena.
sn35.95:10.8 Esevanto dukkhassā”ti.
sn35.95:11.1 “Imassa khvāhaṁ, bhante, bhagavatā saṅkhittena bhāsitassa vitthārena atthaṁ ājānāmi:
sn35.95:12.1 ‘Rūpaṁ disvā sati muṭṭhā,
sn35.95:12.2 Piyaṁ nimittaṁ manasi karoto;
sn35.95:12.3 Sārattacitto vedeti,
sn35.95:12.4 Tañca ajjhosa tiṭṭhati.
sn35.95:13.1 Tassa vaḍḍhanti vedanā,
sn35.95:13.2 anekā rūpasambhavā;
sn35.95:13.3 Abhijjhā ca vihesā ca,
sn35.95:13.4 cittamassūpahaññati;
sn35.95:13.5 Evaṁ ācinato dukkhaṁ,
sn35.95:13.6 ārā nibbāna vuccati.
sn35.95:14.1 Saddaṁ sutvā sati muṭṭhā,
sn35.95:14.2 Piyaṁ nimittaṁ manasi karoto;
sn35.95:14.3 Sārattacitto vedeti,
sn35.95:14.4 Tañca ajjhosa tiṭṭhati.
sn35.95:15.1 Tassa vaḍḍhanti vedanā,
sn35.95:15.2 anekā saddasambhavā;
sn35.95:15.3 Abhijjhā ca vihesā ca,
sn35.95:15.4 cittamassūpahaññati;
sn35.95:15.5 Evaṁ ācinato dukkhaṁ,
sn35.95:15.6 ārā nibbāna vuccati.
sn35.95:16.1 Gandhaṁ ghatvā sati muṭṭhā,
sn35.95:16.2 Piyaṁ nimittaṁ manasi karoto;
sn35.95:16.3 Sārattacitto vedeti,
sn35.95:16.4 Tañca ajjhosa tiṭṭhati.
sn35.95:17.1 Tassa vaḍḍhanti vedanā,
sn35.95:17.2 anekā gandhasambhavā;
sn35.95:17.3 Abhijjhā ca vihesā ca,
sn35.95:17.4 cittamassūpahaññati;
sn35.95:17.5 Evaṁ ācinato dukkhaṁ,
sn35.95:17.6 ārā nibbāna vuccati.
sn35.95:18.1 Rasaṁ bhotvā sati muṭṭhā,
sn35.95:18.2 Piyaṁ nimittaṁ manasi karoto;

sn35.103:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.103
sn35.103:0.2 10. Saḷavagga
sn35.103:0.3 Udakasutta
sn35.103:1.1 “Udako sudaṁ, bhikkhave, rāmaputto evaṁ vācaṁ bhāsati:
sn35.103:1.2 ‘idaṁ jātu vedagū, idaṁ jātu sabbajī, idaṁ jātu apalikhataṁ gaṇḍamūlaṁ palikhaṇin’ti.
sn35.103:1.3 Taṁ kho panetaṁ, bhikkhave, udako rāmaputto avedagūyeva samāno ‘vedagūsmī’ti bhāsati, asabbajīyeva samāno ‘sabbajīsmī’ti bhāsati, apalikhataṁyeva gaṇḍamūlaṁ palikhataṁ me ‘gaṇḍamūlan’ti bhāsati.
sn35.103:1.4 Idha kho taṁ, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sammā vadamāno vadeyya:
sn35.103:1.5 ‘idaṁ jātu vedagū, idaṁ jātu sabbajī, idaṁ jātu apalikhataṁ gaṇḍamūlaṁ palikhaṇin’ti.
sn35.103:2.1 Kathañca, bhikkhave, vedagū hoti?
sn35.103:2.2 Yato kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu channaṁ phassāyatanānaṁ samudayañca atthaṅgamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti;
sn35.103:2.3 evaṁ kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu vedagū hoti.
sn35.103:3.1 Kathañca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sabbajī hoti?
sn35.103:3.2 Yato kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu channaṁ phassāyatanānaṁ samudayañca atthaṅgamañca assādañca ādīnavañca nissaraṇañca yathābhūtaṁ viditvā anupādāvimutto hoti;
sn35.103:3.3 evaṁ kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sabbajī hoti.
sn35.103:4.1 Kathañca, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno apalikhataṁ gaṇḍamūlaṁ palikhataṁ hoti?
sn35.103:4.2 Gaṇḍoti kho, bhikkhave, imassetaṁ cātumahābhūtikassa kāyassa adhivacanaṁ mātāpettikasambhavassa odanakummāsūpacayassa aniccucchādanaparimaddanabhedanaviddhaṁsanadhammassa.
sn35.103:4.3 Gaṇḍamūlanti kho, bhikkhave, taṇhāyetaṁ adhivacanaṁ.
sn35.103:4.4 Yato kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno taṇhā pahīnā hoti ucchinnamūlā tālāvatthukatā anabhāvaṅkatā āyatiṁ anuppādadhammā;
sn35.103:4.5 evaṁ kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno apalikhataṁ gaṇḍamūlaṁ palikhataṁ hoti.
sn35.103:5.1 Udako sudaṁ, bhikkhave, rāmaputto evaṁ vācaṁ bhāsati:
sn35.103:5.2 ‘idaṁ jātu vedagū, idaṁ jātu sabbajī, idaṁ jātu apalikhataṁ gaṇḍamūlaṁ palikhaṇin’ti.
sn35.103:5.3 Taṁ kho panetaṁ, bhikkhave, udako rāmaputto avedagūyeva samāno ‘vedagūsmī’ti bhāsati, asabbajīyeva samāno ‘sabbajīsmī’ti bhāsati;
sn35.103:5.4 apalikhataṁyeva gaṇḍamūlaṁ ‘palikhataṁ me gaṇḍamūlan’ti bhāsati.
sn35.103:5.5 Idha kho taṁ, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sammā vadamāno vadeyya:
sn35.103:5.6 ‘idaṁ jātu vedagū, idaṁ jātu sabbajī, idaṁ jātu apalikhataṁ gaṇḍamūlaṁ palikhaṇin’”ti.
sn35.103:5.7 Dasamaṁ.
sn35.103:5.8 Saḷavaggo pañcamo.
sn35.103:6.0 Tassuddānaṁ
sn35.103:6.1 Dve saṅgayhā parihānaṁ,
sn35.103:6.2 Pamādavihārī ca saṁvaro;
sn35.103:6.3 Samādhi paṭisallānaṁ,
sn35.103:6.4 Dve natumhākena uddakoti.
sn35.103:6.5 Saḷāyatanavagge dutiyapaṇṇāsako samatto.

sn35.116:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.116
sn35.116:0.2 12. Lokakāmaguṇavagga
sn35.116:0.3 Lokantagamanasutta
sn35.116:1.1 “Nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, gamanena lokassa antaṁ ñāteyyaṁ, daṭṭheyyaṁ, patteyyanti vadāmi.
sn35.116:1.2 Na ca panāhaṁ, bhikkhave, appatvā lokassa antaṁ dukkhassa antakiriyaṁ vadāmī”ti.
sn35.116:1.3 Idaṁ vatvā bhagavā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ pāvisi.
sn35.116:1.4 Atha kho tesaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ acirapakkantassa bhagavato etadahosi:
sn35.116:1.5 “idaṁ kho no, āvuso, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.116:1.6 ‘“nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, gamanena lokassa antaṁ ñāteyyaṁ, daṭṭheyyaṁ, patteyyan”ti vadāmi.
sn35.116:1.7 Na ca panāhaṁ, bhikkhave, appatvā lokassa antaṁ dukkhassa antakiriyaṁ vadāmī’ti.
sn35.116:1.8 Ko nu kho imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajeyyā”ti?
sn35.116:2.1 Atha kho tesaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ etadahosi:
sn35.116:2.2 “ayaṁ kho āyasmā ānando satthu ceva saṁvaṇṇito, sambhāvito ca viññūnaṁ sabrahmacārīnaṁ.
sn35.116:2.3 Pahoti cāyasmā ānando imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajituṁ.
sn35.116:2.4 Yannūna mayaṁ yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkameyyāma; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyāmā”ti.
sn35.116:3.1 Atha kho te bhikkhū yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkamiṁsu; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā ānandena saddhiṁ sammodiṁsu.
sn35.116:3.2 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdiṁsu. Ekamantaṁ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etadavocuṁ:
sn35.116:4.1 “Idaṁ kho no, āvuso ānanda, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.116:4.2 ‘nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, gamanena lokassa antaṁ ñāteyyaṁ, daṭṭheyyaṁ, patteyyanti vadāmi.
sn35.116:4.3 Na ca panāhaṁ, bhikkhave, appatvā lokassa antaṁ dukkhassa antakiriyaṁ vadāmī’ti.
sn35.116:4.4 Tesaṁ no, āvuso, amhākaṁ acirapakkantassa bhagavato etadahosi:
sn35.116:4.5 ‘idaṁ kho no, āvuso, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho—
sn35.116:4.6 nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, gamanena lokassa antaṁ ñāteyyaṁ, daṭṭheyyaṁ, patteyyanti vadāmi.
sn35.116:4.7 Na ca panāhaṁ, bhikkhave, appatvā lokassa antaṁ dukkhassa antakiriyaṁ vadāmīti.
sn35.116:4.8 Ko nu kho imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajeyyā’ti?
sn35.116:4.9 Tesaṁ no, āvuso, amhākaṁ etadahosi:
sn35.116:4.10 ‘ayaṁ kho, āvuso, āyasmā ānando satthu ceva saṁvaṇṇito, sambhāvito ca viññūnaṁ sabrahmacārīnaṁ.
sn35.116:4.11 Pahoti cāyasmā ānando imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajituṁ.
sn35.116:4.12 Yannūna mayaṁ yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkameyyāma; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyāmā’ti.
sn35.116:4.13 Vibhajatāyasmā ānando”ti.
sn35.116:5.1 “Seyyathāpi, āvuso, puriso sāratthiko sāragavesī sārapariyesanaṁ caramāno mahato rukkhassa tiṭṭhato sāravato atikkammeva, mūlaṁ atikkammeva, khandhaṁ sākhāpalāse sāraṁ pariyesitabbaṁ maññeyya;
sn35.116:5.2 evaṁ sampadamidaṁ āyasmantānaṁ satthari sammukhībhūte taṁ bhagavantaṁ atisitvā amhe etamatthaṁ paṭipucchitabbaṁ maññatha.
sn35.116:5.3 So hāvuso, bhagavā jānaṁ jānāti, passaṁ passati—
sn35.116:5.4 cakkhubhūto, ñāṇabhūto, dhammabhūto, brahmabhūto, vattā, pavattā, atthassa ninnetā, amatassa dātā, dhammassāmī, tathāgato.
sn35.116:5.5 So ceva panetassa kālo ahosi yaṁ bhagavantaṁyeva etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyātha.
sn35.116:5.6 Yathā vo bhagavā byākareyya tathā vo dhāreyyāthā”ti.
sn35.116:6.1 “Addhāvuso ānanda, bhagavā jānaṁ jānāti, passaṁ passati—
sn35.116:6.2 cakkhubhūto, ñāṇabhūto, dhammabhūto, brahmabhūto, vattā, pavattā, atthassa ninnetā, amatassa dātā, dhammassāmī, tathāgato.
sn35.116:6.3 So ceva panetassa kālo ahosi yaṁ bhagavantaṁyeva etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyāma.
sn35.116:6.4 Yathā no bhagavā byākareyya tathā naṁ dhāreyyāma.
sn35.116:6.5 Api cāyasmā ānando satthu ceva saṁvaṇṇito, sambhāvito ca viññūnaṁ sabrahmacārīnaṁ.
sn35.116:6.6 Pahoti cāyasmā ānando imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajituṁ.
sn35.116:6.7 Vibhajatāyasmā ānando agaruṁ karitvā”ti.
sn35.116:7.1 “Tenahāvuso, suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn35.116:7.2 “Evamāvuso”ti kho te bhikkhū āyasmato ānandassa paccassosuṁ.
sn35.116:7.3 Āyasmā ānando etadavoca:
sn35.116:8.1 “Yaṁ kho vo, āvuso, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.116:8.2 ‘nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, gamanena lokassa antaṁ ñāteyyaṁ, daṭṭheyyaṁ, patteyyanti vadāmi.
sn35.116:8.3 Na ca panāhaṁ, bhikkhave, appatvā lokassa antaṁ dukkhassa antakiriyaṁ vadāmī’ti,
sn35.116:8.4 imassa khvāhaṁ, āvuso, bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ ājānāmi.
sn35.116:8.5 Yena kho, āvuso, lokasmiṁ lokasaññī hoti lokamānī—
sn35.116:8.6 ayaṁ vuccati ariyassa vinaye loko.
sn35.116:8.7 Kena cāvuso, lokasmiṁ lokasaññī hoti lokamānī?
sn35.116:8.8 Cakkhunā kho, āvuso, lokasmiṁ lokasaññī hoti lokamānī.
sn35.116:8.9 Sotena kho, āvuso …
sn35.116:8.10 ghānena kho, āvuso …
sn35.116:8.11 jivhāya kho, āvuso, lokasmiṁ lokasaññī hoti lokamānī.
sn35.116:8.12 Kāyena kho, āvuso …
sn35.116:8.13 manena kho, āvuso, lokasmiṁ lokasaññī hoti lokamānī.
sn35.116:8.14 Yena kho, āvuso, lokasmiṁ lokasaññī hoti lokamānī—
sn35.116:8.15 ayaṁ vuccati ariyassa vinaye loko.
sn35.116:8.16 Yaṁ kho vo, āvuso, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.116:8.17 ‘nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, gamanena lokassa antaṁ ñāteyyaṁ, daṭṭheyyaṁ, patteyyanti vadāmi.
sn35.116:8.18 Na ca panāhaṁ, bhikkhave, appatvā lokassa antaṁ dukkhassa antakiriyaṁ vadāmī’ti,
sn35.116:8.19 imassa khvāhaṁ, āvuso, bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa evaṁ vitthārena atthaṁ ājānāmi.
sn35.116:8.20 Ākaṅkhamānā ca pana tumhe āyasmanto bhagavantaṁyeva upasaṅkamitvā etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyātha.
sn35.116:8.21 Yathā vo bhagavā byākaroti tathā naṁ dhāreyyāthā”ti.
sn35.116:9.1 “Evamāvuso”ti kho te bhikkhū āyasmato ānandassa paṭissutvā uṭṭhāyāsanā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṁsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdiṁsu. Ekamantaṁ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū bhagavantaṁ etadavocuṁ:
sn35.116:10.1 “Yaṁ kho no, bhante, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.116:10.2 ‘nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, gamanena lokassa antaṁ ñāteyyaṁ, daṭṭheyyaṁ, patteyyanti vadāmi.
sn35.116:10.3 Na ca panāhaṁ, bhikkhave, appatvā lokassa antaṁ dukkhassa antakiriyaṁ vadāmī’ti.
sn35.116:10.4 Tesaṁ no, bhante, amhākaṁ acirapakkantassa bhagavato etadahosi:
sn35.116:10.5 ‘idaṁ kho no, āvuso, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho—
sn35.116:10.6 nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, gamanena lokassa antaṁ ñāteyyaṁ, daṭṭheyyaṁ, patteyyanti vadāmi.
sn35.116:10.7 Na ca panāhaṁ, bhikkhave, appatvā lokassa antaṁ dukkhassa antakiriyaṁ vadāmīti.
sn35.116:10.8 Ko nu kho imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajeyyā’ti?
sn35.116:10.9 Tesaṁ no, bhante, amhākaṁ etadahosi:
sn35.116:10.10 ‘ayaṁ kho āyasmā ānando satthu ceva saṁvaṇṇito, sambhāvito ca viññūnaṁ sabrahmacārīnaṁ.
sn35.116:10.11 Pahoti cāyasmā ānando imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajituṁ.
sn35.116:10.12 Yannūna mayaṁ yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkameyyāma; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyāmā’ti.
sn35.116:10.13 Atha kho mayaṁ, bhante, yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkamimha; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etamatthaṁ paṭipucchimha.
sn35.116:10.14 Tesaṁ no, bhante, āyasmatā ānandena imehi ākārehi imehi padehi imehi byañjanehi attho vibhatto”ti.
sn35.116:11.1 “Paṇḍito, bhikkhave, ānando; mahāpañño, bhikkhave, ānando.
sn35.116:11.2 Mañcepi tumhe, bhikkhave, etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyātha, ahampi taṁ evamevaṁ byākareyyaṁ yathā taṁ ānandena byākataṁ.
sn35.116:11.3 Eso cevetassa attho, evañca naṁ dhāreyyāthā”ti.
sn35.116:11.4 Tatiyaṁ. "
sn35.117:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.117
sn35.117:0.2 12. Lokakāmaguṇavagga
sn35.117:0.3 Kāmaguṇasutta
sn35.117:1.1 “Pubbeva me, bhikkhave, sambodhā anabhisambuddhassa bodhisattasseva sato etadahosi:
sn35.117:1.2 ‘yeme pañca kāmaguṇā cetaso samphuṭṭhapubbā atītā niruddhā vipariṇatā, tatra me cittaṁ bahulaṁ gacchamānaṁ gaccheyya paccuppannesu vā appaṁ vā anāgatesu’.
sn35.117:1.3 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi:
sn35.117:1.4 ‘yeme pañca kāmaguṇā cetaso samphuṭṭhapubbā atītā niruddhā vipariṇatā, tatra me attarūpena appamādo sati cetaso ārakkho karaṇīyo’.
sn35.117:1.5 Tasmātiha, bhikkhave, tumhākampi ye te pañca kāmaguṇā cetaso samphuṭṭhapubbā atītā niruddhā vipariṇatā, tatra vo cittaṁ bahulaṁ gacchamānaṁ gaccheyya paccuppannesu vā appaṁ vā anāgatesu.
sn35.117:1.6 Tasmātiha, bhikkhave, tumhākampi ye te pañca kāmaguṇā cetaso samphuṭṭhapubbā atītā niruddhā vipariṇatā, tatra vo attarūpehi appamādo sati cetaso ārakkho karaṇīyo.
sn35.117:1.7 Tasmātiha, bhikkhave, se āyatane veditabbe yattha cakkhu ca nirujjhati, rūpasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:1.8 yattha jivhā ca nirujjhati, rasasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:1.9 yattha mano ca nirujjhati, dhammasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe”ti.
sn35.117:1.10 Idaṁ vatvā bhagavā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ pāvisi.
sn35.117:2.1 Atha kho tesaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ acirapakkantassa bhagavato etadahosi:
sn35.117:2.2 “idaṁ kho no, āvuso, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.117:2.3 ‘tasmātiha, bhikkhave, se āyatane veditabbe yattha cakkhu ca nirujjhati, rūpasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:2.4 yattha jivhā ca nirujjhati, rasasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:2.5 yattha mano ca nirujjhati, dhammasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe’ti.
sn35.117:2.6 Ko nu kho imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajeyyā”ti?
sn35.117:3.1 Atha kho tesaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ etadahosi:
sn35.117:3.2 “ayaṁ kho āyasmā ānando satthu ceva saṁvaṇṇito, sambhāvito ca viññūnaṁ sabrahmacārīnaṁ.
sn35.117:3.3 Pahoti cāyasmā ānando imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajituṁ.
sn35.117:3.4 Yannūna mayaṁ yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkameyyāma; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyāmā”ti.
sn35.117:4.1 Atha kho te bhikkhū yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkamiṁsu; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā ānandena saddhiṁ sammodiṁsu.
sn35.117:4.2 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdiṁsu. Ekamantaṁ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etadavocuṁ:
sn35.117:5.1 “Idaṁ kho no, āvuso ānanda, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.117:5.2 ‘tasmātiha, bhikkhave, se āyatane veditabbe yattha cakkhu ca nirujjhati, rūpasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:5.3 yattha jivhā ca nirujjhati, rasasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:5.4 yattha mano ca nirujjhati, dhammasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe’ti.
sn35.117:5.5 Tesaṁ no, āvuso, amhākaṁ acirapakkantassa bhagavato etadahosi:
sn35.117:5.6 ‘idaṁ kho no, āvuso, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.117:5.7 “tasmātiha, bhikkhave, se āyatane veditabbe yattha cakkhu ca nirujjhati, rūpasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:5.8 yattha jivhā ca nirujjhati, rasasaññā ca nirujjhati se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:5.9 yattha mano ca nirujjhati, dhammasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe”ti.
sn35.117:5.10 Ko nu kho imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajeyyā’ti?
sn35.117:5.11 Tesaṁ no, āvuso, amhākaṁ etadahosi:
sn35.117:5.12 ‘ayaṁ kho āyasmā ānando satthu ceva saṁvaṇṇito, sambhāvito ca viññūnaṁ sabrahmacārīnaṁ.
sn35.117:5.13 Pahoti cāyasmā ānando imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajituṁ.
sn35.117:5.14 Yannūna mayaṁ yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkameyyāma; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyāmā’ti.
sn35.117:5.15 Vibhajatāyasmā ānando”ti.
sn35.117:6.1 “Seyyathāpi, āvuso, puriso sāratthiko sāragavesī sārapariyesanaṁ caramāno mahato rukkhassa …pe…
sn35.117:6.2 vibhajatāyasmā ānando agaruṁ karitvā”ti.
sn35.117:7.1 “Tenahāvuso, suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn35.117:7.2 “Evamāvuso”ti kho te bhikkhū āyasmato ānandassa paccassosuṁ.
sn35.117:7.3 Āyasmā ānando etadavoca:
sn35.117:8.1 “Yaṁ kho vo, āvuso, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.117:8.2 ‘tasmātiha, bhikkhave, se āyatane veditabbe yattha cakkhu ca nirujjhati, rūpasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:8.3 yattha mano ca nirujjhati, dhammasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe’ti.
sn35.117:8.4 Imassa khvāhaṁ, āvuso, bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ ājānāmi.
sn35.117:8.5 Saḷāyatananirodhaṁ no etaṁ, āvuso, bhagavatā sandhāya bhāsitaṁ:
sn35.117:8.6 ‘tasmātiha, bhikkhave, se āyatane veditabbe, yattha cakkhu ca nirujjhati, rūpasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:8.7 yattha mano ca nirujjhati, dhammasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe’ti.
sn35.117:8.8 Ayaṁ kho, āvuso, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.117:8.9 ‘tasmātiha, bhikkhave, se āyatane veditabbe yattha cakkhu ca nirujjhati, rūpasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:8.10 yattha mano ca nirujjhati, dhammasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe’ti.
sn35.117:8.11 Imassa khvāhaṁ, āvuso, bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa evaṁ vitthārena atthaṁ ājānāmi.
sn35.117:8.12 Ākaṅkhamānā ca pana tumhe āyasmanto bhagavantaṁyeva upasaṅkamatha;
sn35.117:8.13 upasaṅkamitvā etamatthaṁ puccheyyātha.
sn35.117:8.14 Yathā vo bhagavā byākaroti tathā naṁ dhāreyyāthā”ti.
sn35.117:9.1 “Evamāvuso”ti kho te bhikkhū āyasmato ānandassa paṭissutvā uṭṭhāyāsanā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṁsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdiṁsu. Ekamantaṁ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū bhagavantaṁ etadavocuṁ:
sn35.117:10.1 “Yaṁ kho no, bhante, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.117:10.2 ‘tasmātiha, bhikkhave, se āyatane veditabbe yattha cakkhu ca nirujjhati, rūpasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:10.3 yattha jivhā ca nirujjhati, rasasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:10.4 yattha mano ca nirujjhati, dhammasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe’ti, tesaṁ no, bhante, amhākaṁ acirapakkantassa bhagavato etadahosi:
sn35.117:10.5 ‘idaṁ kho no, āvuso, bhagavā saṅkhittena uddesaṁ uddisitvā vitthārena atthaṁ avibhajitvā uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ paviṭṭho:
sn35.117:10.6 “tasmātiha, bhikkhave, se āyatane veditabbe yattha cakkhu ca nirujjhati, rūpasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe …pe…
sn35.117:10.7 yattha mano ca nirujjhati, dhammasaññā ca nirujjhati, se āyatane veditabbe”ti.
sn35.117:10.8 Ko nu kho imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajeyyā’ti?
sn35.117:10.9 Tesaṁ no, bhante, amhākaṁ etadahosi:
sn35.117:10.10 ‘ayaṁ kho āyasmā ānando satthu ceva saṁvaṇṇito, sambhāvito ca viññūnaṁ sabrahmacārīnaṁ.
sn35.117:10.11 Pahoti cāyasmā ānando imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena uddesassa uddiṭṭhassa vitthārena atthaṁ avibhattassa vitthārena atthaṁ vibhajituṁ.
sn35.117:10.12 Yannūna mayaṁ yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkameyyāma; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyāmā’ti.
sn35.117:10.13 Atha kho mayaṁ, bhante, yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkamimha; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etamatthaṁ paṭipucchimha.
sn35.117:10.14 Tesaṁ no, bhante, āyasmatā ānandena imehi ākārehi, imehi padehi, imehi byañjanehi attho vibhatto”ti.
sn35.117:11.1 “Paṇḍito, bhikkhave, ānando; mahāpañño, bhikkhave, ānando.
sn35.117:11.2 Mañcepi tumhe, bhikkhave, etamatthaṁ paṭipuccheyyātha, ahampi taṁ evamevaṁ byākareyyaṁ yathā taṁ ānandena byākataṁ.
sn35.117:11.3 Eso cevetassa attho. Evañca naṁ dhāreyyāthā”ti.
sn35.117:11.4 Catutthaṁ. "
sn35.118:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.118
sn35.118:0.2 12. Lokakāmaguṇavagga
sn35.118:0.3 Sakkapañhasutta
sn35.118:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā rājagahe viharati gijjhakūṭe pabbate.
sn35.118:1.2 Atha kho sakko devānamindo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṁ ṭhito kho sakko devānamindo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.118:1.3 “ko nu kho, bhante, hetu, ko paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme no parinibbāyanti?
sn35.118:1.4 Ko pana, bhante, hetu, ko paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme parinibbāyantī”ti?
sn35.118:2.1 “Santi kho, devānaminda, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā, iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.118:2.2 Tañce bhikkhu abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.118:2.3 Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.118:2.4 Saupādāno, devānaminda, bhikkhu no parinibbāyati …pe….
sn35.118:3.1 Santi kho, devānaminda, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe…
sn35.118:3.2 santi kho, devānaminda, manoviññeyyā dhammā, iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.118:3.3 Tañce bhikkhu abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.118:3.4 Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.118:3.5 Saupādāno, devānaminda, bhikkhu no parinibbāyati.
sn35.118:3.6 Ayaṁ kho, devānaminda, hetu, ayaṁ paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme no parinibbāyanti.
sn35.118:4.1 Santi ca kho, devānaminda, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā, iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.118:4.2 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.118:4.3 Tassa taṁ anabhinandato anabhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato na tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti, na tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.118:4.4 Anupādāno, devānaminda, bhikkhu parinibbāyati …pe….
sn35.118:5.1 Santi kho, devānaminda, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe…
sn35.118:5.2 santi kho, devānaminda, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.118:5.3 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.118:5.4 Tassa taṁ anabhinandato anabhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato na tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti na tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.118:5.5 Anupādāno, devānaminda, bhikkhu parinibbāyati.
sn35.118:5.6 Ayaṁ kho, devānaminda, hetu, ayaṁ paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme parinibbāyantī”ti.
sn35.118:5.7 Pañcamaṁ. "
sn35.119:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.119
sn35.119:0.2 12. Lokakāmaguṇavagga
sn35.119:0.3 Pañcasikhasutta
sn35.119:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā rājagahe viharati gijjhakūṭe pabbate.
sn35.119:1.2 Atha kho pañcasikho gandhabbadevaputto yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṁ ṭhito kho pañcasikho gandhabbadevaputto bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.119:1.3 “ko nu kho, bhante, hetu, ko paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme no parinibbāyanti?
sn35.119:1.4 Ko pana, bhante, hetu, ko paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme parinibbāyantī”ti?
sn35.119:1.5 “Santi kho, pañcasikha, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā …pe…
sn35.119:1.6 santi kho, pañcasikha, manoviññeyyā dhammā, iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.119:1.7 Tañce bhikkhu abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.119:1.8 Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.119:1.9 Saupādāno, pañcasikha, bhikkhu no parinibbāyati.
sn35.119:1.10 Ayaṁ kho, pañcasikha, hetu, ayaṁ paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme no parinibbāyanti.
sn35.119:2.1 Santi ca kho, pañcasikha, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā …pe…
sn35.119:2.2 santi kho, pañcasikha, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.119:2.3 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati, tassa taṁ anabhinandato anabhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato na tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti, na tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.119:2.4 Anupādāno, pañcasikha, bhikkhu parinibbāyati.
sn35.119:2.5 Ayaṁ kho, pañcasikha, hetu, ayaṁ paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme parinibbāyantī”ti.

sn35.120:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.120
sn35.120:0.2 12. Lokakāmaguṇavagga
sn35.120:0.3 Sāriputtasaddhivihārikasutta
sn35.120:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ āyasmā sāriputto sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.
sn35.120:1.2 Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yenāyasmā sāriputto tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā sāriputtena saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn35.120:1.3 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho so bhikkhu āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.120:1.4 “saddhivihāriko, āvuso sāriputta, bhikkhu sikkhaṁ paccakkhāya hīnāyāvatto”ti.
sn35.120:2.1 “Evametaṁ, āvuso, hoti indriyesu aguttadvārassa, bhojane amattaññuno, jāgariyaṁ ananuyuttassa.
sn35.120:2.2 ‘So vatāvuso, bhikkhu indriyesu aguttadvāro bhojane amattaññū jāgariyaṁ ananuyutto yāvajīvaṁ paripuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ santānessatī’ti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.
sn35.120:2.3 ‘So vatāvuso, bhikkhu indriyesu guttadvāro, bhojane mattaññū, jāgariyaṁ anuyutto yāvajīvaṁ paripuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ santānessatī’ti ṭhānametaṁ vijjati.
sn35.120:3.1 Kathañcāvuso, indriyesu guttadvāro hoti?
sn35.120:3.2 Idhāvuso, bhikkhu cakkhunā rūpaṁ disvā na nimittaggāhī hoti nānubyañjanaggāhī.
sn35.120:3.3 Yatvādhikaraṇamenaṁ cakkhundriyaṁ asaṁvutaṁ viharantaṁ abhijjhādomanassā pāpakā akusalā dhammā anvāssaveyyuṁ tassa saṁvarāya paṭipajjati, rakkhati cakkhundriyaṁ, cakkhundriye saṁvaraṁ āpajjati.
sn35.120:3.4 Sotena saddaṁ sutvā …
sn35.120:3.5 ghānena gandhaṁ ghāyitvā …
sn35.120:3.6 jivhāya rasaṁ sāyitvā …
sn35.120:3.7 kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṁ phusitvā …
sn35.120:3.8 manasā dhammaṁ viññāya na nimittaggāhī hoti nānubyañjanaggāhī.
sn35.120:3.9 Yatvādhikaraṇamenaṁ manindriyaṁ asaṁvutaṁ viharantaṁ abhijjhādomanassā pāpakā akusalā dhammā anvāssaveyyuṁ, tassa saṁvarāya paṭipajjati, rakkhati manindriyaṁ, manindriye saṁvaraṁ āpajjati.
sn35.120:3.10 Evaṁ kho, āvuso, indriyesu guttadvāro hoti.
sn35.120:4.1 Kathañcāvuso, bhojane mattaññū hoti?
sn35.120:4.2 Idhāvuso, bhikkhu paṭisaṅkhā yoniso āhāraṁ āhāreti:
sn35.120:4.3 ‘neva davāya, na madāya, na maṇḍanāya, na vibhūsanāya, yāvadeva imassa kāyassa ṭhitiyā yāpanāya, vihiṁsūparatiyā, brahmacariyānuggahāya. Iti purāṇañca vedanaṁ paṭihaṅkhāmi, navañca vedanaṁ na uppādessāmi, yātrā ca me bhavissati, anavajjatā ca phāsuvihāro cā’ti.
sn35.120:4.4 Evaṁ kho, āvuso, bhojane mattaññū hoti.
sn35.120:5.1 Kathañcāvuso, jāgariyaṁ anuyutto hoti?
sn35.120:5.2 Idhāvuso, bhikkhu divasaṁ caṅkamena nisajjāya āvaraṇīyehi dhammehi cittaṁ parisodheti.
sn35.120:5.3 Rattiyā paṭhamaṁ yāmaṁ caṅkamena nisajjāya āvaraṇīyehi dhammehi cittaṁ parisodheti.
sn35.120:5.4 Rattiyā majjhimaṁ yāmaṁ dakkhiṇena passena sīhaseyyaṁ kappeti pāde pādaṁ accādhāya sato sampajāno, uṭṭhānasaññaṁ manasi karitvā.
sn35.120:5.5 Rattiyā pacchimaṁ yāmaṁ paccuṭṭhāya caṅkamena nisajjāya āvaraṇīyehi dhammehi cittaṁ parisodheti.
sn35.120:5.6 Evaṁ kho, āvuso, jāgariyaṁ anuyutto hoti.
sn35.120:5.7 Tasmātihāvuso, evaṁ sikkhitabbaṁ:
sn35.120:5.8 ‘indriyesu guttadvārā bhavissāma, bhojane mattaññuno, jāgariyaṁ anuyuttā’ti.
sn35.120:5.9 Evañhi vo, āvuso, sikkhitabban”ti.
sn35.120:5.10 Sattamaṁ. "
sn35.121:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.121
sn35.121:0.2 12. Lokakāmaguṇavagga
sn35.121:0.3 Rāhulovādasutta
sn35.121:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.
sn35.121:1.2 Atha kho bhagavato rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṁ cetaso parivitakko udapādi:
sn35.121:1.3 “paripakkā kho rāhulassa vimuttiparipācaniyā dhammā;
sn35.121:1.4 yannūnāhaṁ rāhulaṁ uttariṁ āsavānaṁ khaye vineyyan”ti.
sn35.121:1.5 Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṁ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiyaṁ piṇḍāya caritvā
sn35.121:1.6 pacchābhattaṁ piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto āyasmantaṁ rāhulaṁ āmantesi:
sn35.121:1.7 “gaṇhāhi, rāhula, nisīdanaṁ.
sn35.121:1.8 Yena andhavanaṁ tenupasaṅkamissāma divāvihārāyā”ti.
sn35.121:1.9 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho āyasmā rāhulo bhagavato paṭissutvā nisīdanaṁ ādāya bhagavantaṁ piṭṭhito piṭṭhito anubandhi.
sn35.121:2.1 Tena kho pana samayena anekāni devatāsahassāni bhagavantaṁ anubandhāni honti:
sn35.121:2.2 “ajja bhagavā āyasmantaṁ rāhulaṁ uttariṁ āsavānaṁ khaye vinessatī”ti.
sn35.121:2.3 Atha kho bhagavā andhavanaṁ ajjhogāhetvā aññatarasmiṁ rukkhamūle paññatte āsane nisīdi.
sn35.121:2.4 Āyasmāpi kho rāhulo bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi.
sn35.121:2.5 Ekamantaṁ nisinnaṁ kho āyasmantaṁ rāhulaṁ bhagavā etadavoca:
sn35.121:3.1 “Taṁ kiṁ maññasi, rāhula,
sn35.121:3.2 cakkhu niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:4.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:5.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vā taṁ sukhaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:6.1 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:7.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ:
sn35.121:7.2 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’”ti?
sn35.121:8.1 “No hetaṁ, bhante”. (…)
sn35.121:9.1 “Rūpā niccā vā aniccā vā”ti?
sn35.121:10.1 “Aniccā, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:11.1 “Cakkhuviññāṇaṁ niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:12.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:13.1 “Cakkhusamphasso nicco vā anicco vā”ti?
sn35.121:14.1 “Anicco, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:15.1 “Yampidaṁ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedanāgataṁ, saññāgataṁ, saṅkhāragataṁ, viññāṇagataṁ, tampi niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:16.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:17.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vā taṁ sukhaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:18.1 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:19.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ:
sn35.121:19.2 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’”ti?
sn35.121:20.1 “No hetaṁ, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:21.1 “Jivhā niccā vā aniccā vā”ti?
sn35.121:22.1 “Aniccā, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:23.1 “Jivhāviññāṇaṁ niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:24.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:25.1 “Jivhāsamphasso nicco vā anicco vā”ti?
sn35.121:26.1 “Anicco, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:27.1 “Yampidaṁ jivhāsamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedanāgataṁ, saññāgataṁ, saṅkhāragataṁ, viññāṇagataṁ, tampi niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:28.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:29.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vā taṁ sukhaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:30.1 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:31.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ:
sn35.121:31.2 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’”ti?
sn35.121:32.1 “No hetaṁ, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:33.1 “Mano nicco vā anicco vā”ti?
sn35.121:34.1 “Anicco, bhante”.
sn35.121:35.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vā taṁ sukhaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:36.1 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:37.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ
sn35.121:37.2 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’”ti?
sn35.121:38.1 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:39.1 “Dhammā niccā vā aniccā vā”ti?
sn35.121:40.1 “Aniccā, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:41.1 “Manoviññāṇaṁ niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:42.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:43.1 “Manosamphasso nicco vā anicco vā”ti?
sn35.121:44.1 “Anicco, bhante” …pe….
sn35.121:45.1 “Yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedanāgataṁ, saññāgataṁ, saṅkhāragataṁ, viññāṇagataṁ, tampi niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:46.1 “Aniccaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:47.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vā taṁ sukhaṁ vā”ti?
sn35.121:48.1 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:49.1 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ:
sn35.121:49.2 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’”ti?
sn35.121:50.1 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.121:51.1 “Evaṁ passaṁ, rāhula, sutavā ariyasāvako cakkhusmimpi nibbindati, rūpesupi nibbindati, cakkhuviññāṇepi nibbindati, cakkhusamphassepi nibbindati, yampidaṁ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedanāgataṁ saññāgataṁ saṅkhāragataṁ viññāṇagataṁ tasmimpi nibbindati …pe…
sn35.121:51.2 jivhāyapi nibbindati, rasesupi nibbindati, jivhāviññāṇepi nibbindati, jivhāsamphassepi nibbindati, yampidaṁ jivhāsamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedanāgataṁ saññāgataṁ saṅkhāragataṁ viññāṇagataṁ tasmimpi nibbindati …pe….
sn35.121:52.1 Manasmimpi nibbindati, dhammesupi nibbindati, manoviññāṇepi nibbindati, manosamphassepi nibbindati, yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedanāgataṁ saññāgataṁ saṅkhāragataṁ viññāṇagataṁ tasmimpi nibbindati.
sn35.121:52.2 Nibbindaṁ virajjati; virāgā vimuccati; vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti.
sn35.121:52.3 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.
sn35.121:53.1 Idamavoca bhagavā.
sn35.121:53.2 Attamano āyasmā rāhulo bhagavato bhāsitaṁ abhinandi.
sn35.121:53.3 Imasmiñca pana veyyākaraṇasmiṁ bhaññamāne āyasmato rāhulassa anupādāya āsavehi cittaṁ vimucci.
sn35.121:53.4 Anekānañca devatāsahassānaṁ virajaṁ vītamalaṁ dhammacakkhuṁ udapādi:
sn35.121:53.5 “yaṁ kiñci samudayadhammaṁ sabbaṁ taṁ nirodhadhamman”ti.
sn35.121:53.6 Aṭṭhamaṁ. "

sn35.122:0.3 Saṁyojaniyadhammasutta
sn35.122:1.1 “Saṁyojaniye ca, bhikkhave, dhamme desessāmi saṁyojanañca.
sn35.122:1.2 Taṁ suṇātha.
sn35.122:1.3 Katame ca, bhikkhave, saṁyojaniyā dhammā, katamañca saṁyojanaṁ?
sn35.122:1.4 Santi, bhikkhave, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.122:1.5 Ime vuccanti, bhikkhave, saṁyojaniyā dhammā.
sn35.122:1.6 Yo tattha chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.122:1.7 santi, bhikkhave, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe…
sn35.122:1.8 santi, bhikkhave, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.122:1.9 Ime vuccanti, bhikkhave, saṁyojaniyā dhammā.
sn35.122:1.10 Yo tattha chandarāgo taṁ tattha saṁyojanan”ti.
sn35.122:1.11 Navamaṁ. "
sn35.123:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.123
sn35.123:0.2 12. Lokakāmaguṇavagga
sn35.123:0.3 Upādāniyadhammasutta
sn35.123:1.1 “Upādāniye ca, bhikkhave, dhamme desessāmi upādānañca.
sn35.123:1.2 Taṁ suṇātha.
sn35.123:1.3 Katame ca, bhikkhave, upādāniyā dhammā, katamañca upādānaṁ?
sn35.123:1.4 Santi, bhikkhave, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.123:1.5 Ime vuccanti, bhikkhave, upādāniyā dhammā.
sn35.123:1.6 Yo tattha chandarāgo, taṁ tattha upādānaṁ …pe…
sn35.123:1.7 santi, bhikkhave, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe…
sn35.123:1.8 santi, bhikkhave, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.123:1.9 Ime vuccanti, bhikkhave, upādāniyā dhammā.
sn35.123:1.10 Yo tattha chandarāgo taṁ tattha upādānan”ti.
sn35.123:1.11 Dasamaṁ.
sn35.123:1.12 Lokakāmaguṇavaggo dutiyo.
sn35.123:2.0 Tassuddānaṁ

sn35.123:2.2 lokakāmaguṇena ca;
sn35.123:2.3 Sakko pañcasikho ceva,
sn35.123:2.4 sāriputto ca rāhulo;
