sn35.124:0.2 13. Gahapativagga
sn35.124:0.3 Vesālīsutta
sn35.124:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā vesāliyaṁ viharati mahāvane kūṭāgārasālāyaṁ.
sn35.124:1.2 Atha kho uggo gahapati vesāliko yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho uggo gahapati vesāliko bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.124:1.3 “ko nu kho, bhante, hetu, ko paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme no parinibbāyanti?
sn35.124:1.4 Ko pana, bhante, hetu, ko paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme parinibbāyantī”ti?
sn35.124:2.1 “Santi kho, gahapati, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.124:2.2 Tañce bhikkhu abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati. Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.124:2.3 Saupādāno, gahapati, bhikkhu no parinibbāyati …pe…
sn35.124:2.4 santi kho, gahapati, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe…
sn35.124:2.5 santi kho, gahapati, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.124:2.6 Tañce bhikkhu abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati. Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.124:2.7 Saupādāno, gahapati, bhikkhu no parinibbāyati.
sn35.124:2.8 Ayaṁ kho, gahapati, hetu, ayaṁ paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme no parinibbāyanti.
sn35.124:3.1 Santi ca kho, gahapati, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā, iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.124:3.2 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati. Tassa taṁ anabhinandato anabhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato na tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti, na tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.124:3.3 Anupādāno, gahapati, bhikkhu parinibbāyati …pe…
sn35.124:3.4 santi kho, gahapati, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe…
sn35.124:3.5 santi kho, gahapati, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.124:3.6 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati, tassa taṁ anabhinandato anabhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato. Na tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti, na tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.124:3.7 Anupādāno, gahapati, bhikkhu parinibbāyati.
sn35.124:3.8 Ayaṁ kho, gahapati, hetu ayaṁ paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme parinibbāyantī”ti.
sn35.124:3.9 Paṭhamaṁ. "

sn35.127:0.2 13. Gahapativagga
sn35.127:0.3 Bhāradvājasutta
sn35.127:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ āyasmā piṇḍolabhāradvājo kosambiyaṁ viharati ghositārāme.
sn35.127:1.2 Atha kho rājā udeno yenāyasmā piṇḍolabhāradvājo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā piṇḍolabhāradvājena saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn35.127:1.3 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho rājā udeno āyasmantaṁ piṇḍolabhāradvājaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.127:1.4 “ko nu kho, bho bhāradvāja, hetu ko paccayo yenime daharā bhikkhū susū kāḷakesā bhadrena yobbanena samannāgatā paṭhamena vayasā anikīḷitāvino kāmesu yāvajīvaṁ paripuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ caranti, addhānañca āpādentī”ti?
sn35.127:1.5 “Vuttaṁ kho etaṁ, mahārāja, tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena:
sn35.127:1.6 ‘etha tumhe, bhikkhave, mātumattīsu mātucittaṁ upaṭṭhapetha, bhaginimattīsu bhaginicittaṁ upaṭṭhapetha, dhītumattīsu dhītucittaṁ upaṭṭhapethā’ti.
sn35.127:1.7 Ayaṁ kho, mahārāja, hetu, ayaṁ paccayo yenime daharā bhikkhū susū kāḷakesā bhadrena yobbanena samannāgatā paṭhamena vayasā anikīḷitāvino kāmesu yāvajīvaṁ paripuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ caranti, addhānañca āpādentī”ti.
sn35.127:2.1 “Lolaṁ kho, bho bhāradvāja, cittaṁ.
sn35.127:2.2 Appekadā mātumattīsupi lobhadhammā uppajjanti, bhaginimattīsupi lobhadhammā uppajjanti, dhītumattīsupi lobhadhammā uppajjanti.
sn35.127:2.3 Atthi nu kho, bho bhāradvāja, añño ca hetu, añño ca paccayo yenime daharā bhikkhū susū kāḷakesā …pe… addhānañca āpādentī”ti?
sn35.127:3.1 “Vuttaṁ kho etaṁ, mahārāja, tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena:
sn35.127:3.2 ‘etha tumhe, bhikkhave, imameva kāyaṁ uddhaṁ pādatalā adho kesamatthakā tacapariyantaṁ pūraṁ nānappakārassa asucino paccavekkhatha—
sn35.127:3.3 atthi imasmiṁ kāye kesā lomā nakhā dantā taco maṁsaṁ nhāru aṭṭhi aṭṭhimiñjaṁ vakkaṁ hadayaṁ yakanaṁ kilomakaṁ pihakaṁ papphāsaṁ antaṁ antaguṇaṁ udariyaṁ karīsaṁ pittaṁ semhaṁ pubbo lohitaṁ sedo medo assu vasā kheḷo siṅghāṇikā lasikā muttan’ti.
sn35.127:3.4 Ayampi kho, mahārāja, hetu, ayaṁ paccayo yenime daharā bhikkhū susū kāḷakesā …pe… addhānañca āpādentī”ti.
sn35.127:3.5 “Ye te, bho bhāradvāja, bhikkhū bhāvitakāyā bhāvitasīlā bhāvitacittā bhāvitapaññā, tesaṁ taṁ sukaraṁ hoti.
sn35.127:3.6 Ye ca kho te, bho bhāradvāja, bhikkhū abhāvitakāyā abhāvitasīlā abhāvitacittā abhāvitapaññā, tesaṁ taṁ dukkaraṁ hoti.
sn35.127:3.7 Appekadā, bho bhāradvāja, asubhato manasi karissāmīti subhatova āgacchati.
sn35.127:3.8 Atthi nu kho, bho bhāradvāja, añño ca kho hetu añño ca paccayo yenime daharā bhikkhū susū kāḷakesā …pe… addhānañca āpādentī”ti?
sn35.127:4.1 “Vuttaṁ kho etaṁ, mahārāja, tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena:
sn35.127:4.2 ‘etha tumhe, bhikkhave, indriyesu guttadvārā viharatha.
sn35.127:4.3 Cakkhunā rūpaṁ disvā mā nimittaggāhino ahuvattha, mānubyañjanaggāhino.
sn35.127:4.4 Yatvādhikaraṇamenaṁ cakkhundriyaṁ asaṁvutaṁ viharantaṁ abhijjhādomanassā pāpakā akusalā dhammā anvāssaveyyuṁ, tassa saṁvarāya paṭipajjatha. Rakkhatha cakkhundriyaṁ; cakkhundriye saṁvaraṁ āpajjatha.
sn35.127:4.5 Sotena saddaṁ sutvā …pe…
sn35.127:4.6 ghānena gandhaṁ ghāyitvā …
sn35.127:4.7 jivhāya rasaṁ sāyitvā …
sn35.127:4.8 kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṁ phusitvā …
sn35.127:4.9 manasā dhammaṁ viññāya mā nimittaggāhino ahuvattha, mānubyañjanaggāhino.
sn35.127:4.10 Yatvādhikaraṇamenaṁ manindriyaṁ asaṁvutaṁ viharantaṁ abhijjhādomanassā pāpakā akusalā dhammā anvāssaveyyuṁ, tassa saṁvarāya paṭipajjatha. Rakkhatha manindriyaṁ; manindriye saṁvaraṁ āpajjathā’ti.
sn35.127:4.11 Ayampi kho, mahārāja, hetu ayaṁ paccayo yenime daharā bhikkhū susū kāḷakesā bhadrena yobbanena samannāgatā paṭhamena vayasā anikīḷitāvino kāmesu yāvajīvaṁ paripuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ caranti, addhānañca āpādentī”ti.
sn35.127:5.1 “Acchariyaṁ, bho bhāradvāja; abbhutaṁ, bho bhāradvāja.
sn35.127:5.2 Yāva subhāsitañcidaṁ, bho bhāradvāja, tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena.
sn35.127:5.3 Esova kho, bho bhāradvāja, hetu, esa paccayo yenime daharā bhikkhū susū kāḷakesā bhadrena yobbanena samannāgatā paṭhamena vayasā anikīḷitāvino kāmesu yāvajīvaṁ paripuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ caranti, addhānañca āpādentīti.
sn35.127:5.4 Ahampi kho, bho bhāradvāja, yasmiṁ samaye arakkhiteneva kāyena, arakkhitāya vācāya, arakkhitena cittena, anupaṭṭhitāya satiyā, asaṁvutehi indriyehi antepuraṁ pavisāmi, ativiya maṁ tasmiṁ samaye lobhadhammā parisahanti.
sn35.127:5.5 Yasmiñca khvāhaṁ, bho bhāradvāja, samaye rakkhiteneva kāyena, rakkhitāya vācāya, rakkhitena cittena, upaṭṭhitāya satiyā, saṁvutehi indriyehi antepuraṁ pavisāmi, na maṁ tathā tasmiṁ samaye lobhadhammā parisahanti.
sn35.127:5.6 Abhikkantaṁ, bho bhāradvāja, abhikkantaṁ, bho bhāradvāja.
sn35.127:5.7 Seyyathāpi, bho bhāradvāja, nikkujjitaṁ vā ukkujjeyya, paṭicchannaṁ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṁ ācikkheyya, andhakāre vā telapajjotaṁ dhāreyya: ‘cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantī’ti; evamevaṁ bhotā bhāradvājena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito.
sn35.127:5.8 Esāhaṁ, bho bhāradvāja, taṁ bhagavantaṁ saraṇaṁ gacchāmi, dhammañca, bhikkhusaṅghañca.
sn35.127:5.9 Upāsakaṁ maṁ bhavaṁ bhāradvājo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṁ saraṇaṁ gatan”ti.
sn35.127:5.10 Catutthaṁ. "

sn35.129:1.12 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati sukhā vedanā.
sn35.129:1.13 Saṁvijjati kho, gahapati, jivhādhātu, rasā ca amanāpā, jivhāviññāṇañca dukkhavedaniyaṁ.
sn35.129:1.14 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati dukkhā vedanā.
sn35.129:1.15 Saṁvijjati kho, gahapati, jivhādhātu, rasā ca upekkhāvedaniyā, jivhāviññāṇañca adukkhamasukhavedaniyaṁ.
sn35.129:1.16 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati adukkhamasukhā vedanā …pe…

sn35.129:1.18 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati sukhā vedanā.
sn35.129:1.19 Saṁvijjati kho, gahapati, manodhātu, dhammā ca amanāpā, manoviññāṇañca dukkhavedaniyaṁ.

sn35.129:1.22 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati adukkhamasukhā vedanā.

sn35.130:0.2 13. Gahapativagga
sn35.130:0.3 Hāliddikānisutta
sn35.130:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ āyasmā mahākaccāno avantīsu viharati kuraraghare papāte pabbate.
sn35.130:1.2 Atha kho hāliddikāni gahapati yenāyasmā mahākaccāno tenupasaṅkami …pe… ekamantaṁ nisinno kho hāliddikāni gahapati āyasmantaṁ mahākaccānaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.130:1.3 “vuttamidaṁ, bhante, bhagavatā:
sn35.130:1.4 ‘dhātunānattaṁ paṭicca uppajjati phassanānattaṁ; phassanānattaṁ paṭicca uppajjati vedanānānattan’ti.
sn35.130:1.5 Kathaṁ nu kho, bhante, dhātunānattaṁ paṭicca uppajjati phassanānattaṁ; phassanānattaṁ paṭicca uppajjati vedanānānattan”ti?
sn35.130:1.6 “Idha, gahapati, bhikkhu cakkhunā rūpaṁ disvā ‘manāpaṁ itthetan’ti pajānāti cakkhuviññāṇaṁ sukhavedaniyañca.
sn35.130:1.7 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati sukhā vedanā.
sn35.130:1.8 Cakkhunā kho paneva rūpaṁ disvā ‘amanāpaṁ itthetan’ti pajānāti cakkhuviññāṇaṁ dukkhavedaniyañca.
sn35.130:1.9 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati dukkhā vedanā.
sn35.130:1.10 Cakkhunā kho paneva rūpaṁ disvā ‘upekkhāṭṭhāniyaṁ itthetan’ti pajānāti cakkhuviññāṇaṁ adukkhamasukhavedaniyañca.
sn35.130:1.11 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati adukkhamasukhā vedanā.
sn35.130:2.1 Puna caparaṁ, gahapati, bhikkhu sotena saddaṁ sutvā …pe…
sn35.130:2.2 ghānena gandhaṁ ghāyitvā …pe…
sn35.130:2.3 jivhāya rasaṁ sāyitvā …pe…
sn35.130:2.4 kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṁ phusitvā …pe…
sn35.130:2.5 manasā dhammaṁ viññāya ‘manāpaṁ itthetan’ti pajānāti manoviññāṇaṁ sukhavedaniyañca.
sn35.130:2.6 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati sukhā vedanā.
sn35.130:2.7 Manasā kho paneva dhammaṁ viññāya ‘amanāpaṁ itthetan’ti pajānāti manoviññāṇaṁ dukkhavedaniyañca.
sn35.130:2.8 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati dukkhā vedanā.
sn35.130:2.9 Manasā kho paneva dhammaṁ viññāya ‘upekkhāṭṭhāniyaṁ itthetan’ti pajānāti manoviññāṇaṁ adukkhamasukhavedaniyañca.
sn35.130:2.10 Phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati adukkhamasukhā vedanā.
sn35.130:2.11 Evaṁ kho, gahapati, dhātunānattaṁ paṭicca uppajjati phassanānattaṁ; phassanānattaṁ paṭicca uppajjati vedanānānattan”ti.
sn35.130:2.12 Sattamaṁ. "
sn35.131:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.131
sn35.131:0.2 13. Gahapativagga
sn35.131:0.3 Nakulapitusutta
sn35.131:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā bhaggesu viharati susumāragire bhesakaḷāvane migadāye.
sn35.131:1.2 Atha kho nakulapitā gahapati yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami …pe… ekamantaṁ nisinno kho nakulapitā gahapati bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.131:1.3 “ko nu kho, bhante, hetu, ko paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme no parinibbāyanti?
sn35.131:1.4 Ko pana, bhante, hetu, ko paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme parinibbāyantī”ti?
sn35.131:1.5 “Santi kho, gahapati, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.131:1.6 Tañce bhikkhu abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.131:1.7 Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.131:1.8 Saupādāno, gahapati, bhikkhu no parinibbāyati …pe…
sn35.131:1.9 santi kho, gahapati, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe…
sn35.131:1.10 santi kho, gahapati, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.131:1.11 Tañce bhikkhu abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.131:1.12 Tassa taṁ abhinandato abhivadato ajjhosāya tiṭṭhato tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.131:1.13 Saupādāno, gahapati, bhikkhu no parinibbāyati.
sn35.131:1.14 Ayaṁ kho, gahapati, hetu ayaṁ paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme no parinibbāyanti.
sn35.131:2.1 Santi ca kho, gahapati, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.131:2.2 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.131:2.3 Tassa taṁ anabhinandato anabhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato na tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti, na tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.131:2.4 Anupādāno, gahapati, bhikkhu parinibbāyati …pe…
sn35.131:2.5 santi kho, gahapati, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe…
sn35.131:2.6 santi kho, gahapati, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.131:2.7 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.131:2.8 Tassa taṁ nābhinandato nābhivadato anajjhosāya tiṭṭhato na tannissitaṁ viññāṇaṁ hoti na tadupādānaṁ.
sn35.131:2.9 Anupādāno, gahapati, bhikkhu parinibbāyati.
sn35.131:2.10 Ayaṁ kho, gahapati, hetu, ayaṁ paccayo yena m’idhekacce sattā diṭṭheva dhamme parinibbāyantī”ti.
sn35.131:2.11 Aṭṭhamaṁ. "
sn35.132:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.132
sn35.132:0.2 13. Gahapativagga
sn35.132:0.3 Lohiccasutta
sn35.132:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ āyasmā mahākaccāno avantīsu viharati makkarakate araññakuṭikāyaṁ.
sn35.132:1.2 Atha kho lohiccassa brāhmaṇassa sambahulā antevāsikā kaṭṭhahārakā māṇavakā yenāyasmato mahākaccānassa araññakuṭikā tenupasaṅkamiṁsu; upasaṅkamitvā parito parito kuṭikāya anucaṅkamanti anuvicaranti uccāsaddā mahāsaddā kānici kānici seleyyakāni karonti:
sn35.132:1.3 “ime pana muṇḍakā samaṇakā ibbhā kaṇhā bandhupādāpaccā, imesaṁ bharatakānaṁ sakkatā garukatā mānitā pūjitā apacitā”ti.
sn35.132:1.4 Atha kho āyasmā mahākaccāno vihārā nikkhamitvā te māṇavake etadavoca:
sn35.132:1.5 “mā māṇavakā saddamakattha;
sn35.132:1.6 dhammaṁ vo bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn35.132:1.7 Evaṁ vutte, te māṇavakā tuṇhī ahesuṁ.
sn35.132:1.8 Atha kho āyasmā mahākaccāno te māṇavake gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi:
sn35.132:2.1 “Sīluttamā pubbatarā ahesuṁ,
sn35.132:2.2 Te brāhmaṇā ye purāṇaṁ saranti;
sn35.132:2.3 Guttāni dvārāni surakkhitāni,
sn35.132:2.4 Ahesuṁ tesaṁ abhibhuyya kodhaṁ.
sn35.132:3.1 Dhamme ca jhāne ca ratā ahesuṁ,
sn35.132:3.2 Te brāhmaṇā ye purāṇaṁ saranti.
sn35.132:4.1 Ime ca vokkamma japāmaseti,
sn35.132:4.2 Gottena mattā visamaṁ caranti;
sn35.132:4.3 Kodhābhibhūtā puthuattadaṇḍā,
sn35.132:4.4 Virajjamānā sataṇhātaṇhesu.
sn35.132:5.1 Aguttadvārassa bhavanti moghā,
sn35.132:5.2 Supineva laddhaṁ purisassa vittaṁ;
sn35.132:5.3 Anāsakā thaṇḍilasāyikā ca,
sn35.132:5.4 Pāto sinānañca tayo ca vedā.
sn35.132:6.1 Kharājinaṁ jaṭāpaṅko,
sn35.132:6.2 mantā sīlabbataṁ tapo;
sn35.132:6.3 Kuhanā vaṅkadaṇḍā ca,
sn35.132:6.4 udakācamanāni ca;
sn35.132:6.5 Vaṇṇā ete brāhmaṇānaṁ,
sn35.132:6.6 katā kiñcikkhabhāvanā.
sn35.132:7.1 Cittañca susamāhitaṁ,
sn35.132:7.2 vippasannamanāvilaṁ;
sn35.132:7.3 Akhilaṁ sabbabhūtesu,
sn35.132:7.4 so maggo brahmapattiyā”ti.
sn35.132:8.1 Atha kho te māṇavakā kupitā anattamanā yena lohicco brāhmaṇo tenupasaṅkamiṁsu; upasaṅkamitvā lohiccaṁ brāhmaṇaṁ etadavocuṁ:
sn35.132:8.2 “yagghe bhavaṁ jāneyya, samaṇo mahākaccāno brāhmaṇānaṁ mante ekaṁsena apavadati, paṭikkosatī”ti?
sn35.132:8.3 Evaṁ vutte, lohicco brāhmaṇo kupito ahosi anattamano.
sn35.132:8.4 Atha kho lohiccassa brāhmaṇassa etadahosi:
sn35.132:8.5 “na kho pana metaṁ patirūpaṁ yohaṁ aññadatthu māṇavakānaṁyeva sutvā samaṇaṁ mahākaccānaṁ akkoseyyaṁ paribhāseyyaṁ.
sn35.132:8.6 Yannūnāhaṁ upasaṅkamitvā puccheyyan”ti.
sn35.132:9.1 Atha kho lohicco brāhmaṇo tehi māṇavakehi saddhiṁ yenāyasmā mahākaccāno tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā mahākaccānena saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn35.132:9.2 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho lohicco brāhmaṇo āyasmantaṁ mahākaccānaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.132:9.3 “āgamaṁsu nu khvidha, bho kaccāna, amhākaṁ sambahulā antevāsikā kaṭṭhahārakā māṇavakā”ti?
sn35.132:9.4 “Āgamaṁsu khvidha te, brāhmaṇa, sambahulā antevāsikā kaṭṭhahārakā māṇavakā”ti.
sn35.132:9.5 “Ahu pana bhoto kaccānassa tehi māṇavakehi saddhiṁ kocideva kathāsallāpo”ti?
sn35.132:9.6 “Ahu kho me, brāhmaṇa, tehi māṇavakehi saddhiṁ kocideva kathāsallāpo”ti.
sn35.132:9.7 “Yathā kathaṁ pana bhoto kaccānassa tehi māṇavakehi saddhiṁ ahosi kathāsallāpo”ti?
sn35.132:9.8 “Evaṁ kho me, brāhmaṇa, tehi māṇavakehi saddhiṁ ahosi kathāsallāpo:
sn35.132:10.1 ‘Sīluttamā pubbatarā ahesuṁ,
sn35.132:10.2 Te brāhmaṇā ye purāṇaṁ saranti;
sn35.132:10.3 …pe…
sn35.132:10.4 Akhilaṁ sabbabhūtesu,
sn35.132:10.5 So maggo brahmapattiyā’ti.
sn35.132:11.1 Evaṁ kho me, brāhmaṇa, tehi māṇavakehi saddhiṁ ahosi kathāsallāpo”ti.
sn35.132:12.1 “‘Aguttadvāro’ti bhavaṁ kaccāno āha.
sn35.132:12.2 Kittāvatā nu kho, bho kaccāna, aguttadvāro hotī”ti?
sn35.132:12.3 “Idha, brāhmaṇa, ekacco cakkhunā rūpaṁ disvā piyarūpe rūpe adhimuccati, appiyarūpe rūpe byāpajjati, anupaṭṭhitakāyassati ca viharati, parittacetaso
sn35.132:12.4 tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti.
sn35.132:12.5 Sotena saddaṁ sutvā …
sn35.132:12.6 ghānena gandhaṁ ghāyitvā …
sn35.132:12.7 jivhāya rasaṁ sāyitvā …
sn35.132:12.8 kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṁ phusitvā …
sn35.132:12.9 manasā dhammaṁ viññāya piyarūpe dhamme adhimuccati, appiyarūpe ca dhamme byāpajjati, anupaṭṭhitakāyassati ca viharati, parittacetaso
sn35.132:12.10 tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ nappajānāti yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti.
sn35.132:12.11 Evaṁ kho, brāhmaṇa, aguttadvāro hotī”ti.
sn35.132:12.12 “Acchariyaṁ, bho kaccāna, abbhutaṁ, bho kaccāna.
sn35.132:12.13 Yāvañcidaṁ bhotā kaccānena aguttadvārova samāno aguttadvāroti akkhāto.
sn35.132:13.1 ‘Guttadvāro’ti bhavaṁ kaccāno āha.
sn35.132:13.2 Kittāvatā nu kho, bho kaccāna, guttadvāro hotī”ti?
sn35.132:13.3 “Idha, brāhmaṇa, bhikkhu cakkhunā rūpaṁ disvā piyarūpe rūpe nādhimuccati, appiyarūpe rūpe na byāpajjati, upaṭṭhitakāyassati ca viharati, appamāṇacetaso
sn35.132:13.4 tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti.
sn35.132:13.5 Sotena saddaṁ sutvā …
sn35.132:13.6 ghānena gandhaṁ ghāyitvā …
sn35.132:13.7 jivhāya rasaṁ sāyitvā …
sn35.132:13.8 kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṁ phusitvā …
sn35.132:13.9 manasā dhammaṁ viññāya piyarūpe dhamme nādhimuccati, appiyarūpe dhamme na byāpajjati, upaṭṭhitakāyassati ca viharati, appamāṇacetaso
sn35.132:13.10 tañca cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, yatthassa te uppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā aparisesā nirujjhanti.
sn35.132:13.11 Evaṁ kho, brāhmaṇa, guttadvāro hotī”ti.
sn35.132:14.1 “Acchariyaṁ, bho kaccāna, abbhutaṁ, bho kaccāna.
sn35.132:14.2 Yāvañcidaṁ bhotā kaccānena guttadvārova samāno guttadvāroti akkhāto.
sn35.132:14.3 Abhikkantaṁ, bho kaccāna; abhikkantaṁ, bho kaccāna.
sn35.132:14.4 Seyyathāpi, bho kaccāna, nikkujjitaṁ vā ukkujjeyya, paṭicchannaṁ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṁ ācikkheyya, andhakāre vā telapajjotaṁ dhāreyya: ‘cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantī’ti; evamevaṁ bhotā kaccānena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito.
sn35.132:14.5 Esāhaṁ, bho kaccāna, taṁ bhagavantaṁ saraṇaṁ gacchāmi, dhammañca, bhikkhusaṅghañca.
sn35.132:14.6 Upāsakaṁ maṁ bhavaṁ kaccāno dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṁ saraṇaṁ gataṁ.
sn35.132:14.7 Yathā ca bhavaṁ kaccāno makkarakate upāsakakulāni upasaṅkamati; evameva lohiccakulaṁ upasaṅkamatu.
sn35.132:14.8 Tattha ye māṇavakā vā māṇavikā vā bhavantaṁ kaccānaṁ abhivādessanti paccuṭṭhissanti āsanaṁ vā udakaṁ vā dassanti, tesaṁ taṁ bhavissati dīgharattaṁ hitāya sukhāyā”ti.
sn35.132:14.9 Navamaṁ. "
sn35.133:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.133
sn35.133:0.2 13. Gahapativagga
sn35.133:0.3 Verahaccānisutta
sn35.133:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ āyasmā udāyī kāmaṇḍāyaṁ viharati todeyyassa brāhmaṇassa ambavane.
sn35.133:1.2 Atha kho verahaccānigottāya brāhmaṇiyā antevāsī māṇavako yenāyasmā udāyī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā udāyinā saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn35.133:1.3 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi.
sn35.133:1.4 Ekamantaṁ nisinnaṁ kho taṁ māṇavakaṁ āyasmā udāyī dhammiyā kathāya sandassesi samādapesi samuttejesi sampahaṁsesi.
sn35.133:1.5 Atha kho so māṇavako āyasmatā udāyinā dhammiyā kathāya sandassito samādapito samuttejito sampahaṁsito uṭṭhāyāsanā yena verahaccānigottā brāhmaṇī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā verahaccānigottaṁ brāhmaṇiṁ etadavoca:
sn35.133:1.6 “yagghe, bhoti, jāneyyāsi.
sn35.133:1.7 Samaṇo udāyī dhammaṁ deseti ādikalyāṇaṁ majjhekalyāṇaṁ pariyosānakalyāṇaṁ, sātthaṁ sabyañjanaṁ kevalaparipuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ pakāsetī”ti.
sn35.133:2.1 “Tena hi tvaṁ, māṇavaka, mama vacanena samaṇaṁ udāyiṁ nimantehi svātanāya bhattenā”ti.
sn35.133:2.2 “Evaṁ, bhotī”ti kho so māṇavako verahaccānigottāya brāhmaṇiyā paṭissutvā yenāyasmā udāyī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ udāyiṁ etadavoca:
sn35.133:2.3 “adhivāsetu kira, bhavaṁ udāyī amhākaṁ ācariyabhariyāya verahaccānigottāya brāhmaṇiyā svātanāya bhattan”ti.
sn35.133:2.4 Adhivāsesi kho āyasmā udāyī tuṇhībhāvena.
sn35.133:2.5 Atha kho āyasmā udāyī tassā rattiyā accayena pubbaṇhasamayaṁ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena verahaccānigottāya brāhmaṇiyā nivesanaṁ tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi.
sn35.133:2.6 Atha kho verahaccānigottā brāhmaṇī āyasmantaṁ udāyiṁ paṇītena khādanīyena bhojanīyena sahatthā santappesi sampavāresi.
sn35.133:2.7 Atha kho verahaccānigottā brāhmaṇī āyasmantaṁ udāyiṁ bhuttāviṁ onītapattapāṇiṁ pādukā ārohitvā ucce āsane nisīditvā sīsaṁ oguṇṭhitvā āyasmantaṁ udāyiṁ etadavoca:
sn35.133:2.8 “bhaṇa, samaṇa, dhamman”ti.
sn35.133:2.9 “Bhavissati, bhagini, samayo”ti vatvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkami.
sn35.133:3.1 Dutiyampi kho so māṇavako yenāyasmā udāyī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā udāyinā saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn35.133:3.2 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi.
sn35.133:3.3 Ekamantaṁ nisinnaṁ kho taṁ māṇavakaṁ āyasmā udāyī dhammiyā kathāya sandassesi samādapesi samuttejesi sampahaṁsesi.
sn35.133:3.4 Dutiyampi kho so māṇavako āyasmatā udāyinā dhammiyā kathāya sandassito samādapito samuttejito sampahaṁsito uṭṭhāyāsanā yena verahaccānigottā brāhmaṇī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā verahaccānigottaṁ brāhmaṇiṁ etadavoca:
sn35.133:3.5 “yagghe, bhoti, jāneyyāsi.
sn35.133:3.6 Samaṇo udāyī dhammaṁ deseti ādikalyāṇaṁ majjhekalyāṇaṁ pariyosānakalyāṇaṁ, sātthaṁ sabyañjanaṁ kevalaparipuṇṇaṁ parisuddhaṁ brahmacariyaṁ pakāsetī”ti.
sn35.133:4.1 “Evamevaṁ pana tvaṁ, māṇavaka, samaṇassa udāyissa vaṇṇaṁ bhāsasi.
sn35.133:4.2 Samaṇo panudāyī ‘bhaṇa, samaṇa, dhamman’ti vutto samāno ‘bhavissati, bhagini, samayo’ti vatvā uṭṭhāyāsanā pakkanto”ti.
sn35.133:4.3 “Tathā hi pana tvaṁ, bhoti, pādukā ārohitvā ucce āsane nisīditvā sīsaṁ oguṇṭhitvā etadavoca:
sn35.133:4.4 ‘bhaṇa, samaṇa, dhamman’ti.
sn35.133:4.5 Dhammagaruno hi te bhavanto dhammagāravā”ti.
sn35.133:4.6 “Tena hi tvaṁ, māṇavaka, mama vacanena samaṇaṁ udāyiṁ nimantehi svātanāya bhattenā”ti.
sn35.133:4.7 “Evaṁ, bhotī”ti kho so māṇavako verahaccānigottāya brāhmaṇiyā paṭissutvā yenāyasmā udāyī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ udāyiṁ etadavoca:
sn35.133:4.8 “adhivāsetu kira bhavaṁ udāyī amhākaṁ ācariyabhariyāya verahaccānigottāya brāhmaṇiyā svātanāya bhattan”ti.
sn35.133:4.9 Adhivāsesi kho āyasmā udāyī tuṇhībhāvena.
sn35.133:5.1 Atha kho āyasmā udāyī tassā rattiyā accayena pubbaṇhasamayaṁ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena verahaccānigottāya brāhmaṇiyā nivesanaṁ tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi.
sn35.133:5.2 Atha kho verahaccānigottā brāhmaṇī āyasmantaṁ udāyiṁ paṇītena khādanīyena bhojanīyena sahatthā santappesi sampavāresi.
sn35.133:5.3 Atha kho verahaccānigottā brāhmaṇī āyasmantaṁ udāyiṁ bhuttāviṁ onītapattapāṇiṁ pādukā orohitvā nīce āsane nisīditvā sīsaṁ vivaritvā āyasmantaṁ udāyiṁ etadavoca:
sn35.133:5.4 “kismiṁ nu kho, bhante, sati arahanto sukhadukkhaṁ paññapenti, kismiṁ asati arahanto sukhadukkhaṁ na paññapentī”ti?
sn35.133:6.1 “Cakkhusmiṁ kho, bhagini, sati arahanto sukhadukkhaṁ paññapenti, cakkhusmiṁ asati arahanto sukhadukkhaṁ na paññapenti …pe…
sn35.133:6.2 jivhāya sati arahanto sukhadukkhaṁ paññapenti, jivhāya asati arahanto sukhadukkhaṁ na paññapenti …pe….

sn35.134:0.3 Devadahasutta
sn35.134:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sakkesu viharati devadahaṁ nāma sakyānaṁ nigamo.
sn35.134:1.2 Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi:
sn35.134:1.3 “nāhaṁ, bhikkhave, sabbesaṁyeva bhikkhūnaṁ chasu phassāyatanesu appamādena karaṇīyanti vadāmi, na ca panāhaṁ, bhikkhave, sabbesaṁyeva bhikkhūnaṁ chasu phassāyatanesu nāppamādena karaṇīyanti vadāmi.
sn35.134:1.4 Ye te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū arahanto khīṇāsavā vusitavanto katakaraṇīyā ohitabhārā anuppattasadatthā parikkhīṇabhavasaṁyojanā sammadaññāvimuttā, tesāhaṁ, bhikkhave, bhikkhūnaṁ chasu phassāyatanesu nāppamādena karaṇīyanti vadāmi.
sn35.134:1.5 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn35.134:1.6 Kataṁ tesaṁ appamādena, abhabbā te pamajjituṁ.
sn35.134:1.7 Ye ca kho te, bhikkhave, bhikkhū sekkhā appattamānasā anuttaraṁ yogakkhemaṁ patthayamānā viharanti, tesāhaṁ, bhikkhave, bhikkhūnaṁ chasu phassāyatanesu appamādena karaṇīyanti vadāmi.
sn35.134:1.8 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn35.134:1.9 Santi, bhikkhave, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā manoramāpi, amanoramāpi.
sn35.134:1.10 Tyāssa phussa phussa cittaṁ na pariyādāya tiṭṭhanti.
sn35.134:1.11 Cetaso apariyādānā āraddhaṁ hoti vīriyaṁ asallīnaṁ, upaṭṭhitā sati asammuṭṭhā, passaddho kāyo asāraddho, samāhitaṁ cittaṁ ekaggaṁ.
sn35.134:1.12 Imaṁ khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, appamādaphalaṁ sampassamāno tesaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ chasu phassāyatanesu appamādena karaṇīyanti vadāmi …pe…
sn35.134:1.13 santi, bhikkhave, manoviññeyyā dhammā manoramāpi amanoramāpi.
sn35.134:1.14 Tyāssa phussa phussa cittaṁ na pariyādāya tiṭṭhanti.
sn35.134:1.15 Cetaso apariyādānā āraddhaṁ hoti vīriyaṁ asallīnaṁ, upaṭṭhitā sati asammuṭṭhā, passaddho kāyo asāraddho, samāhitaṁ cittaṁ ekaggaṁ.
sn35.134:1.16 Imaṁ khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, appamādaphalaṁ sampassamāno tesaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ chasu phassāyatanesu appamādena karaṇīyanti vadāmī”ti.

sn35.152:1.5 Sace pana vo, bhikkhave, aññatitthiyā paribbājakā evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:

sn35.152:1.7 Evaṁ puṭṭhā tumhe, bhikkhave, tesaṁ aññatitthiyānaṁ paribbājakānaṁ evaṁ byākareyyātha:

sn35.152:2.3 Rūpā dukkhā;
sn35.152:2.4 tesaṁ pariññāya bhagavati brahmacariyaṁ vussati.
sn35.152:2.5 Cakkhuviññāṇaṁ dukkhaṁ;
sn35.152:2.6 tassa pariññāya bhagavati brahmacariyaṁ vussati.
sn35.152:2.7 Cakkhusamphasso dukkho;

sn35.152:2.9 Yampidaṁ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi dukkhaṁ;
sn35.152:2.10 tassa pariññāya bhagavati brahmacariyaṁ vussati …pe…
sn35.152:2.11 jivhā dukkhā …
sn35.152:2.12 mano dukkho;
sn35.152:2.13 tassa pariññāya bhagavati brahmacariyaṁ vussati …
sn35.152:2.14 yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi dukkhaṁ;
sn35.152:2.15 tassa pariññāya bhagavati brahmacariyaṁ vussati.
sn35.152:2.16 Idaṁ kho, āvuso, dukkhaṁ;

sn35.153:0.2 15. Navapurāṇavagga
sn35.153:0.3 Atthinukhopariyāyasutta
sn35.153:1.1 “Atthi nu kho, bhikkhave, pariyāyo yaṁ pariyāyaṁ āgamma bhikkhu aññatreva saddhāya, aññatra ruciyā, aññatra anussavā, aññatra ākāraparivitakkā, aññatra diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā aññaṁ byākareyya:
sn35.153:1.2 ‘khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānāmī”ti?
sn35.153:1.3 “Bhagavaṁmūlakā no, bhante, dhammā, bhagavaṁnettikā bhagavaṁpaṭisaraṇā. Sādhu vata, bhante, bhagavantaṁyeva paṭibhātu etassa bhāsitassa attho. Bhagavato sutvā bhikkhū dhāressantī”ti.
sn35.153:1.4 “Tena hi, bhikkhave, suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn35.153:1.5 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn35.153:1.6 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn35.153:1.7 “atthi, bhikkhave, pariyāyo yaṁ pariyāyaṁ āgamma bhikkhu aññatreva saddhāya, aññatra ruciyā, aññatra anussavā, aññatra ākāraparivitakkā, aññatra diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā aññaṁ byākareyya:
sn35.153:1.8 ‘“khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā”ti pajānāmī’ti.
sn35.153:2.1 Katamo ca, bhikkhave, pariyāyo, yaṁ pariyāyaṁ āgamma bhikkhu aññatreva saddhāya …pe… aññatra diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā aññaṁ byākaroti: ‘khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyāti pajānāmī’ti?
sn35.153:2.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu cakkhunā rūpaṁ disvā santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohaṁ, atthi me ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohoti pajānāti;
sn35.153:2.3 asantaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohaṁ, natthi me ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohoti pajānāti.
sn35.153:2.4 Yaṁ taṁ, bhikkhave, bhikkhu cakkhunā rūpaṁ disvā santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohaṁ, atthi me ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohoti pajānāti; asantaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohaṁ, natthi me ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohoti pajānāti. Api nu me, bhikkhave, dhammā saddhāya vā veditabbā, ruciyā vā veditabbā, anussavena vā veditabbā, ākāraparivitakkena vā veditabbā, diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā vā veditabbā”ti?
sn35.153:2.5 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.153:2.6 “Nanume, bhikkhave, dhammā paññāya disvā veditabbā”ti?
sn35.153:2.7 “Evaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.153:2.8 “Ayaṁ kho, bhikkhave, pariyāyo yaṁ pariyāyaṁ āgamma bhikkhu aññatreva saddhāya, aññatra ruciyā, aññatra anussavā, aññatra ākāraparivitakkā, aññatra diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā aññaṁ byākaroti:
sn35.153:2.9 ‘“khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā”ti pajānāmī’ti …pe….
sn35.153:3.1 Puna caparaṁ, bhikkhave, bhikkhu jivhāya rasaṁ sāyitvā santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ …pe… rāgadosamohoti pajānāti; asantaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohaṁ, natthi me ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohoti pajānāti.
sn35.153:3.2 Yaṁ taṁ, bhikkhave, jivhāya rasaṁ sāyitvā santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohaṁ, atthi me ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohoti pajānāti; asantaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohaṁ, natthi me ajjhattaṁ rāgadosamohoti pajānāti; api nu me, bhikkhave, dhammā saddhāya vā veditabbā, ruciyā vā veditabbā, anussavena vā veditabbā, ākāraparivitakkena vā veditabbā, diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā vā veditabbā”ti?
sn35.153:3.3 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.153:3.4 “Nanume, bhikkhave, dhammā paññāya disvā veditabbā”ti?
sn35.153:3.5 “Evaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.153:3.6 “Ayampi kho, bhikkhave, pariyāyo yaṁ pariyāyaṁ āgamma bhikkhu aññatreva saddhāya, aññatra ruciyā, aññatra anussavā, aññatra ākāraparivitakkā, aññatra diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā aññaṁ byākaroti: ‘“khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā”ti pajānāmī’ti …pe….

sn35.229:0.3 Dutiyasamuddasutta
sn35.229:1.1 “‘Samuddo, samuddo’ti, bhikkhave, assutavā puthujjano bhāsati.
sn35.229:1.2 Neso, bhikkhave, ariyassa vinaye samuddo.
sn35.229:1.3 Mahā eso, bhikkhave, udakarāsi mahāudakaṇṇavo.
sn35.229:1.4 Santi, bhikkhave, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.229:1.5 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, ariyassa vinaye samuddo.
sn35.229:1.6 Etthāyaṁ sadevako loko samārako sabrahmako sassamaṇabrāhmaṇī pajā sadevamanussā yebhuyyena samunnā tantākulakajātā kulagaṇṭhikajātā muñjapabbajabhūtā, apāyaṁ duggatiṁ vinipātaṁ saṁsāraṁ nātivattati …pe….
sn35.229:2.1 Santi, bhikkhave, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe… santi, bhikkhave, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.229:2.2 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, ariyassa vinaye samuddo.
sn35.229:2.3 Etthāyaṁ sadevako loko samārako sabrahmako sassamaṇabrāhmaṇī pajā sadevamanussā yebhuyyena samunnā tantākulakajātā kulagaṇṭhikajātā muñjapabbajabhūtā apāyaṁ duggatiṁ vinipātaṁ saṁsāraṁ nātivattatīti.

sn35.230:0.3 Bāḷisikopamasutta
sn35.230:1.1 “Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, bāḷisiko āmisagatabaḷisaṁ gambhīre udakarahade pakkhipeyya.
sn35.230:1.2 Tamenaṁ aññataro āmisacakkhu maccho gileyya.
sn35.230:1.3 Evañhi so, bhikkhave, maccho gilitabaḷiso bāḷisikassa anayaṁ āpanno byasanaṁ āpanno yathākāmakaraṇīyo bāḷisikassa.
sn35.230:2.1 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, chayime baḷisā lokasmiṁ anayāya sattānaṁ vadhāya pāṇinaṁ.
sn35.230:2.2 Katame cha?
sn35.230:2.3 Santi, bhikkhave, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.230:2.4 Tañce, bhikkhu, abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.230:2.5 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, bhikkhu gilitabaḷiso, mārassa anayaṁ āpanno byasanaṁ āpanno yathākāmakaraṇīyo pāpimato …pe…
sn35.230:2.6 santi, bhikkhave, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe….
sn35.230:3.1 Santi, bhikkhave, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.230:3.2 Tañce, bhikkhu, abhinandati abhivadati ajjhosāya tiṭṭhati.
sn35.230:3.3 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, bhikkhu gilitabaḷiso mārassa anayaṁ āpanno byasanaṁ āpanno yathākāmakaraṇīyo pāpimato.
sn35.230:4.1 Santi ca, bhikkhave, cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.230:4.2 Tañce, bhikkhu, nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati. Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na gilitabaḷiso mārassa abhedi baḷisaṁ paribhedi baḷisaṁ na anayaṁ āpanno na byasanaṁ āpanno na yathākāmakaraṇīyo pāpimato …pe….
sn35.230:5.1 Santi, bhikkhave, jivhāviññeyyā rasā …pe….
sn35.230:5.2 Santi, bhikkhave, manoviññeyyā dhammā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṁhitā rajanīyā.
sn35.230:5.3 Tañce bhikkhu nābhinandati nābhivadati nājjhosāya tiṭṭhati, ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na gilitabaḷiso mārassa abhedi baḷisaṁ paribhedi baḷisaṁ na anayaṁ āpanno na byasanaṁ āpanno na yathākāmakaraṇīyo pāpimato”ti.

sn35.231:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.231
sn35.231:0.2 18. Samuddavagga
sn35.231:0.3 Khīrarukkhopamasutta
sn35.231:1.1 “Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā cakkhuviññeyyesu rūpesu yo rāgo so atthi, yo doso so atthi, yo moho so atthi, yo rāgo so appahīno, yo doso so appahīno, yo moho so appahīno tassa parittā cepi cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā cakkhussa āpāthaṁ āgacchanti pariyādiyantevassa cittaṁ; ko pana vādo adhimattānaṁ.
sn35.231:1.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn35.231:1.3 Yo, bhikkhave, rāgo, so atthi, yo doso so atthi, yo moho so atthi, yo rāgo so appahīno, yo doso so appahīno, yo moho so appahīno …pe….
sn35.231:2.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā jivhāviññeyyesu rasesu yo rāgo so atthi …pe….
sn35.231:3.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā manoviññeyyesu dhammesu yo rāgo so atthi, yo doso so atthi, yo moho so atthi, yo rāgo so appahīno, yo doso so appahīno, yo moho so appahīno, tassa parittā cepi manoviññeyyā dhammā manassa āpāthaṁ āgacchanti pariyādiyantevassa cittaṁ; ko pana vādo adhimattānaṁ.
sn35.231:3.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn35.231:3.3 Yo, bhikkhave, rāgo, so atthi, yo doso so atthi, yo moho so atthi, yo rāgo so appahīno, yo doso so appahīno, yo moho so appahīno.
sn35.231:4.1 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, khīrarukkho assattho vā nigrodho vā pilakkho vā udumbaro vā daharo taruṇo komārako.
sn35.231:4.2 Tamenaṁ puriso tiṇhāya kuṭhāriyā yato yato ābhindeyya āgaccheyya khīran”ti?
sn35.231:4.3 “Evaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.231:4.4 “Taṁ kissa hetu”?
sn35.231:4.5 “Yañhi, bhante, khīraṁ taṁ atthī”ti.
sn35.231:5.1 “Evameva kho, bhikkhave, yassa kassaci bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā cakkhuviññeyyesu rūpesu yo rāgo so atthi, yo doso so atthi, yo moho so atthi, yo rāgo so appahīno, yo doso so appahīno, yo moho so appahīno, tassa parittā cepi cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā cakkhussa āpāthaṁ āgacchanti pariyādiyantevassa cittaṁ; ko pana vādo adhimattānaṁ.
sn35.231:5.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn35.231:5.3 Yo, bhikkhave, rāgo so atthi, yo doso so atthi, yo moho so atthi, yo rāgo so appahīno, yo doso so appahīno, yo moho so appahīno …pe….
sn35.231:6.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā jivhāviññeyyesu rasesu yo rāgo so atthi …pe….
sn35.231:7.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā manoviññeyyesu dhammesu yo rāgo so atthi, yo doso so atthi, yo moho so atthi, yo rāgo so appahīno, yo doso so appahīno, yo moho so appahīno, tassa parittā cepi manoviññeyyā dhammā manassa āpāthaṁ āgacchanti pariyādiyantevassa cittaṁ; ko pana vādo adhimattānaṁ.
sn35.231:7.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn35.231:7.3 Yo, bhikkhave, rāgo so atthi, yo doso so atthi, yo moho so atthi, yo rāgo so appahīno, yo doso so appahīno, yo moho so appahīno.
sn35.231:8.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā cakkhuviññeyyesu rūpesu yo rāgo so natthi, yo doso so natthi, yo moho so natthi, yo rāgo so pahīno, yo doso so pahīno, yo moho so pahīno, tassa adhimattā cepi cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā cakkhussa āpāthaṁ āgacchanti nevassa cittaṁ pariyādiyanti; ko pana vādo parittānaṁ.
sn35.231:8.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn35.231:8.3 Yo, bhikkhave, rāgo so natthi, yo doso so natthi, yo moho so natthi, yo rāgo so pahīno, yo doso so pahīno, yo moho so pahīno …pe….
sn35.231:9.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā jivhāviññeyyesu rasesu …pe… manoviññeyyesu dhammesu yo rāgo so natthi, yo doso so natthi, yo moho so natthi, yo rāgo so pahīno, yo doso so pahīno, yo moho so pahīno, tassa adhimattā cepi manoviññeyyā dhammā manassa āpāthaṁ āgacchanti nevassa cittaṁ pariyādiyanti; ko pana vādo parittānaṁ.
sn35.231:9.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn35.231:9.3 Yo, bhikkhave, rāgo so natthi, yo doso so natthi, yo moho so natthi, yo rāgo so pahīno, yo doso so pahīno, yo moho so pahīno.
sn35.231:9.4 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, khīrarukkho assattho vā nigrodho vā pilakkho vā udumbaro vā sukkho kolāpo terovassiko.
sn35.231:9.5 Tamenaṁ puriso tiṇhāya kuṭhāriyā yato yato ābhindeyya āgaccheyya khīran”ti?
sn35.231:9.6 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn35.231:9.7 “Taṁ kissa hetu”?
sn35.231:9.8 “Yañhi, bhante, khīraṁ taṁ natthī”ti.
sn35.231:10.1 “Evameva kho, bhikkhave, yassa kassaci bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā cakkhuviññeyyesu rūpesu yo rāgo so natthi, yo doso so natthi, yo moho so natthi, yo rāgo so pahīno, yo doso so pahīno, yo moho so pahīno, tassa adhimattā cepi cakkhuviññeyyā rūpā cakkhussa āpāthaṁ āgacchanti nevassa cittaṁ pariyādiyanti; ko pana vādo parittānaṁ.
sn35.231:10.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn35.231:10.3 Yo, bhikkhave, rāgo so natthi, yo doso so natthi, yo moho so natthi, yo rāgo so pahīno, yo doso so pahīno, yo moho so pahīno …pe….
sn35.231:11.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā jivhāviññeyyesu rasesu …pe….
sn35.231:12.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa vā bhikkhuniyā vā manoviññeyyesu dhammesu yo rāgo so natthi, yo doso so natthi, yo moho so natthi, yo rāgo so pahīno, yo doso so pahīno, yo moho so pahīno, tassa adhimattā cepi manoviññeyyā dhammā manassa āpāthaṁ āgacchanti, nevassa cittaṁ pariyādiyanti; ko pana vādo parittānaṁ.

sn35.232:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.232
sn35.232:0.2 18. Samuddavagga
sn35.232:0.3 Koṭṭhikasutta
sn35.232:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ āyasmā ca sāriputto āyasmā ca mahākoṭṭhiko bārāṇasiyaṁ viharanti isipatane migadāye.
sn35.232:1.2 Atha kho āyasmā mahākoṭṭhiko sāyanhasamayaṁ paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā sāriputto tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā sāriputtena saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn35.232:1.3 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā mahākoṭṭhiko āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.232:2.1 “Kiṁ nu kho, āvuso sāriputta, cakkhu rūpānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, rūpā cakkhussa saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.232:2.2 jivhā rasānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, rasā jivhāya saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.232:2.3 mano dhammānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, dhammā manassa saṁyojanan”ti?
sn35.232:3.1 “Na kho, āvuso koṭṭhika, cakkhu rūpānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rūpā cakkhussa saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:3.2 Yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.232:3.3 na jivhā rasānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rasā jivhāya saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:3.4 Yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.232:3.5 na mano dhammānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na dhammā manassa saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:3.6 Yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:4.1 Seyyathāpi, āvuso, kāḷo ca balībaddo odāto ca balībaddo ekena dāmena vā yottena vā saṁyuttā assu.
sn35.232:4.2 Yo nu kho evaṁ vadeyya:
sn35.232:4.3 ‘kāḷo balībaddo odātassa balībaddassa saṁyojanaṁ, odāto balībaddo kāḷassa balībaddassa saṁyojanan’ti, sammā nu kho so vadamāno vadeyyā”ti?
sn35.232:4.4 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn35.232:4.5 “Na kho, āvuso, kāḷo balībaddo odātassa balībaddassa saṁyojanaṁ, na odāto balībaddo kāḷassa balībaddassa saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:4.6 Yena ca kho te ekena dāmena vā yottena vā saṁyuttā taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:5.1 Evameva kho, āvuso, na cakkhu rūpānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rūpā cakkhussa saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:5.2 Yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.232:5.3 na jivhā rasānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.232:5.4 na mano dhammānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na dhammā manassa saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:5.5 Yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:6.1 Cakkhu vā, āvuso, rūpānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ abhavissa, rūpā vā cakkhussa saṁyojanaṁ, nayidaṁ brahmacariyavāso paññāyetha sammā dukkhakkhayāya.
sn35.232:6.2 Yasmā ca kho, āvuso, na cakkhu rūpānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rūpā cakkhussa saṁyojanaṁ;
sn35.232:6.3 yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ, tasmā brahmacariyavāso paññāyati sammā dukkhakkhayāya …pe….
sn35.232:7.1 Jivhā, āvuso, rasānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ abhavissa, rasā vā jivhāya saṁyojanaṁ, nayidaṁ brahmacariyavāso paññāyetha sammā dukkhakkhayāya.
sn35.232:7.2 Yasmā ca kho, āvuso, na jivhā rasānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rasā jivhāya saṁyojanaṁ; yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ, tasmā brahmacariyavāso paññāyati sammā dukkhakkhayāya …pe….
sn35.232:8.1 Mano vā, āvuso, dhammānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ abhavissa, dhammā vā manassa saṁyojanaṁ, nayidaṁ brahmacariyavāso paññāyetha sammā dukkhakkhayāya.
sn35.232:8.2 Yasmā ca kho, āvuso, na mano dhammānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na dhammā manassa saṁyojanaṁ;
sn35.232:8.3 yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ, tasmā brahmacariyavāso paññāyati sammā dukkhakkhayāya.
sn35.232:9.1 Imināpetaṁ, āvuso, pariyāyena veditabbaṁ yathā na cakkhu rūpānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rūpā cakkhussa saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:9.2 Yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.232:9.3 na jivhā rasānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.232:9.4 na mano dhammānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na dhammā manassa saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:9.5 Yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:10.1 Saṁvijjati kho, āvuso, bhagavato cakkhu.
sn35.232:10.2 Passati bhagavā cakkhunā rūpaṁ.
sn35.232:10.3 Chandarāgo bhagavato natthi.
sn35.232:10.4 Suvimuttacitto bhagavā.
sn35.232:10.5 Saṁvijjati kho, āvuso, bhagavato sotaṁ.
sn35.232:10.6 Suṇāti bhagavā sotena saddaṁ.
sn35.232:10.7 Chandarāgo bhagavato natthi.
sn35.232:10.8 Suvimuttacitto bhagavā.
sn35.232:10.9 Saṁvijjati kho, āvuso, bhagavato ghānaṁ.
sn35.232:10.10 Ghāyati bhagavā ghānena gandhaṁ.
sn35.232:10.11 Chandarāgo bhagavato natthi.
sn35.232:10.12 Suvimuttacitto bhagavā.
sn35.232:10.13 Saṁvijjati kho, āvuso, bhagavato jivhā.
sn35.232:10.14 Sāyati bhagavā jivhāya rasaṁ.
sn35.232:10.15 Chandarāgo bhagavato natthi.
sn35.232:10.16 Suvimuttacitto bhagavā.
sn35.232:10.17 Saṁvijjati kho, āvuso, bhagavato kāyo.
sn35.232:10.18 Phusati bhagavā kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṁ.
sn35.232:10.19 Chandarāgo bhagavato natthi.
sn35.232:10.20 Suvimuttacitto bhagavā.
sn35.232:10.21 Saṁvijjati kho, āvuso, bhagavato mano.
sn35.232:10.22 Vijānāti bhagavā manasā dhammaṁ.
sn35.232:10.23 Chandarāgo bhagavato natthi.
sn35.232:10.24 Suvimuttacitto bhagavā.
sn35.232:11.1 Iminā kho etaṁ, āvuso, pariyāyena veditabbaṁ yathā na cakkhu rūpānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rūpā cakkhussa saṁyojanaṁ;
sn35.232:11.2 yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:11.3 Na sotaṁ …
sn35.232:11.4 na ghānaṁ …
sn35.232:11.5 na jivhā rasānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rasā jivhāya saṁyojanaṁ;
sn35.232:11.6 yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.232:11.7 Na kāyo …
sn35.232:11.8 na mano dhammānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na dhammā manassa saṁyojanaṁ;
sn35.232:11.9 yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanan”ti.
sn35.232:11.10 Pañcamaṁ. "
sn35.233:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.233
sn35.233:0.2 18. Samuddavagga
sn35.233:0.3 Kāmabhūsutta
sn35.233:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ āyasmā ca ānando āyasmā ca kāmabhū kosambiyaṁ viharanti ghositārāme.
sn35.233:1.2 Atha kho āyasmā kāmabhū sāyanhasamayaṁ paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā ānandena saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn35.233:1.3 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā kāmabhū āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.233:2.1 “Kiṁ nu kho, āvuso ānanda, cakkhu rūpānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, rūpā cakkhussa saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.233:2.2 jivhā rasānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, rasā jivhāya saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.233:2.3 mano dhammānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, dhammā manassa saṁyojanan”ti?
sn35.233:3.1 “Na kho, āvuso kāmabhū, cakkhu rūpānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rūpā cakkhussa saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.233:3.2 Yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.233:3.3 na jivhā rasānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rasā jivhāya saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.233:3.4 na mano dhammānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na dhammā manassa saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.233:3.5 Yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.233:4.1 Seyyathāpi, āvuso, kāḷo ca balībaddo odāto ca balībaddo ekena dāmena vā yottena vā saṁyuttā assu.
sn35.233:4.2 Yo nu kho evaṁ vadeyya:
sn35.233:4.3 ‘kāḷo balībaddo odātassa balībaddassa saṁyojanaṁ, odāto balībaddo kāḷassa balībaddassa saṁyojanan’ti, sammā nu kho so vadamāno vadeyyā”ti?
sn35.233:4.4 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn35.233:4.5 “Na kho, āvuso, kāḷo balībaddo odātassa balībaddassa saṁyojanaṁ, napi odāto balībaddo kāḷassa balībaddassa saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.233:4.6 Yena ca kho te ekena dāmena vā yottena vā saṁyuttā, taṁ tattha saṁyojanaṁ.
sn35.233:4.7 Evameva kho, āvuso, na cakkhu rūpānaṁ saṁyojanaṁ, na rūpā cakkhussa saṁyojanaṁ …pe…
sn35.233:4.8 na jivhā …pe…
sn35.233:4.9 na mano …pe…
sn35.233:4.10 yañca tattha tadubhayaṁ paṭicca uppajjati chandarāgo, taṁ tattha saṁyojanan”ti.
sn35.233:4.11 Chaṭṭhaṁ. "
sn35.234:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.234
sn35.234:0.2 18. Samuddavagga
sn35.234:0.3 Udāyīsutta
sn35.234:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ āyasmā ca ānando āyasmā ca udāyī kosambiyaṁ viharanti ghositārāme.
sn35.234:1.2 Atha kho āyasmā udāyī sāyanhasamayaṁ paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā ānandena saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn35.234:1.3 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā udāyī āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etadavoca:
sn35.234:2.1 “Yatheva nu kho, āvuso ānanda, ayaṁ kāyo bhagavatā anekapariyāyena akkhāto vivaṭo pakāsito:
sn35.234:2.2 ‘itipāyaṁ kāyo anattā’ti, sakkā evameva viññāṇaṁ pidaṁ ācikkhituṁ desetuṁ paññapetuṁ paṭṭhapetuṁ vivarituṁ vibhajituṁ uttānīkātuṁ: ‘itipidaṁ viññāṇaṁ anattā’”ti?
sn35.234:3.1 “Yatheva kho, āvuso udāyī, ayaṁ kāyo bhagavatā anekapariyāyena akkhāto vivaṭo pakāsito:
sn35.234:3.2 ‘itipāyaṁ kāyo anattā’ti, sakkā evameva viññāṇaṁ pidaṁ ācikkhituṁ desetuṁ paññapetuṁ paṭṭhapetuṁ vivarituṁ vibhajituṁ uttānīkātuṁ: ‘itipidaṁ viññāṇaṁ anattā’”ti.
sn35.234:4.1 “Cakkhuñca, āvuso, paṭicca rūpe ca uppajjati cakkhuviññāṇan”ti?
sn35.234:4.2 “Evamāvuso”ti.
sn35.234:4.3 “Yo cāvuso, hetu, yo ca paccayo cakkhuviññāṇassa uppādāya, so ca hetu, so ca paccayo sabbena sabbaṁ sabbathā sabbaṁ aparisesaṁ nirujjheyya. Api nu kho cakkhuviññāṇaṁ paññāyethā”ti?
sn35.234:4.4 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn35.234:4.5 “Imināpi kho etaṁ, āvuso, pariyāyena bhagavatā akkhātaṁ vivaṭaṁ pakāsitaṁ: ‘itipidaṁ viññāṇaṁ anattā’”ti …pe….
sn35.234:5.1 “Jivhañcāvuso, paṭicca rase ca uppajjati jivhāviññāṇan”ti?
sn35.234:5.2 “Evamāvuso”ti.
sn35.234:5.3 “Yo cāvuso, hetu yo ca paccayo jivhāviññāṇassa uppādāya, so ca hetu, so ca paccayo sabbena sabbaṁ sabbathā sabbaṁ aparisesaṁ nirujjheyya, api nu kho jivhāviññāṇaṁ paññāyethā”ti?
sn35.234:5.4 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn35.234:5.5 “Imināpi kho etaṁ, āvuso, pariyāyena bhagavatā akkhātaṁ vivaṭaṁ pakāsitaṁ: ‘itipidaṁ viññāṇaṁ anattā’”ti …pe….
sn35.234:6.1 “Manañcāvuso, paṭicca dhamme ca uppajjati manoviññāṇan”ti?
sn35.234:6.2 “Evamāvuso”ti.
sn35.234:6.3 “Yo cāvuso, hetu, yo ca paccayo manoviññāṇassa uppādāya, so ca hetu, so ca paccayo sabbena sabbaṁ sabbathā sabbaṁ aparisesaṁ nirujjheyya, api nu kho manoviññāṇaṁ paññāyethā”ti?
sn35.234:6.4 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn35.234:6.5 “Imināpi kho etaṁ, āvuso, pariyāyena bhagavatā akkhātaṁ vivaṭaṁ pakāsitaṁ: ‘itipidaṁ viññāṇaṁ anattā’ti.
sn35.234:7.1 Seyyathāpi, āvuso, puriso sāratthiko sāragavesī sārapariyesanaṁ caramāno tiṇhaṁ kuṭhāriṁ ādāya vanaṁ paviseyya. So tattha passeyya mahantaṁ kadalikkhandhaṁ ujuṁ navaṁ akukkukajātaṁ. Tamenaṁ mūle chindeyya; mūle chetvā agge chindeyya; agge chetvā pattavaṭṭiṁ vinibbhujeyya. So tattha pheggumpi nādhigaccheyya, kuto sāraṁ.
sn35.234:7.2 Evameva kho, āvuso, bhikkhu chasu phassāyatanesu nevattānaṁ na attaniyaṁ samanupassati.
sn35.234:7.3 So evaṁ asamanupassanto na kiñci loke upādiyati.
sn35.234:7.4 Anupādiyaṁ na paritassati. Aparitassaṁ paccattaññeva parinibbāyati.
sn35.234:7.5 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.
sn35.234:7.6 Sattamaṁ. "
sn35.235:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 35.235
sn35.235:0.2 18. Samuddavagga
sn35.235:0.3 Ādittapariyāyasutta
sn35.235:1.1 “Ādittapariyāyaṁ vo, bhikkhave, dhammapariyāyaṁ desessāmi.
sn35.235:1.2 Taṁ suṇātha.
sn35.235:1.3 Katamo ca, bhikkhave, ādittapariyāyo, dhammapariyāyo?
sn35.235:1.4 Varaṁ, bhikkhave, tattāya ayosalākāya ādittāya sampajjalitāya sajotibhūtāya cakkhundriyaṁ sampalimaṭṭhaṁ, na tveva cakkhuviññeyyesu rūpesu anubyañjanaso nimittaggāho.
sn35.235:1.5 Nimittassādagathitaṁ vā, bhikkhave, viññāṇaṁ tiṭṭhamānaṁ tiṭṭheyya, anubyañjanassādagathitaṁ vā tasmiñce samaye kālaṁ kareyya, ṭhānametaṁ vijjati, yaṁ dvinnaṁ gatīnaṁ aññataraṁ gatiṁ gaccheyya—
sn35.235:1.6 nirayaṁ vā, tiracchānayoniṁ vā.
sn35.235:1.7 Imaṁ khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, ādīnavaṁ disvā evaṁ vadāmi.
sn35.235:2.1 Varaṁ, bhikkhave, tiṇhena ayosaṅkunā ādittena sampajjalitena sajotibhūtena sotindriyaṁ sampalimaṭṭhaṁ, na tveva sotaviññeyyesu saddesu anubyañjanaso nimittaggāho.
sn35.235:2.2 Nimittassādagathitaṁ vā, bhikkhave, viññāṇaṁ tiṭṭhamānaṁ tiṭṭheyya, anubyañjanassādagathitaṁ vā tasmiñce samaye kālaṁ kareyya, ṭhānametaṁ vijjati, yaṁ dvinnaṁ gatīnaṁ aññataraṁ gatiṁ gaccheyya—
sn35.235:2.3 nirayaṁ vā tiracchānayoniṁ vā.
sn35.235:2.4 Imaṁ khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, ādīnavaṁ disvā evaṁ vadāmi.
sn35.235:3.1 Varaṁ, bhikkhave, tiṇhena nakhacchedanena ādittena sampajjalitena sajotibhūtena ghānindriyaṁ sampalimaṭṭhaṁ, na tveva ghānaviññeyyesu gandhesu anubyañjanaso nimittaggāho.
sn35.235:3.2 Nimittassādagathitaṁ vā, bhikkhave, viññāṇaṁ tiṭṭhamānaṁ tiṭṭheyya, anubyañjanassādagathitaṁ vā tasmiñce samaye kālaṁ kareyya.
sn35.235:3.3 Ṭhānametaṁ vijjati, yaṁ dvinnaṁ gatīnaṁ aññataraṁ gatiṁ gaccheyya—
sn35.235:3.4 nirayaṁ vā tiracchānayoniṁ vā.
sn35.235:3.5 Imaṁ khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, ādīnavaṁ disvā evaṁ vadāmi.
sn35.235:4.1 Varaṁ, bhikkhave, tiṇhena khurena ādittena sampajjalitena sajotibhūtena jivhindriyaṁ sampalimaṭṭhaṁ, na tveva jivhāviññeyyesu rasesu anubyañjanaso nimittaggāho.
sn35.235:4.2 Nimittassādagathitaṁ vā, bhikkhave, viññāṇaṁ tiṭṭhamānaṁ tiṭṭheyya, anubyañjanassādagathitaṁ vā tasmiñce samaye kālaṁ kareyya.
sn35.235:4.3 Ṭhānametaṁ vijjati, yaṁ dvinnaṁ gatīnaṁ aññataraṁ gatiṁ gaccheyya—
sn35.235:4.4 nirayaṁ vā tiracchānayoniṁ vā.
sn35.235:4.5 Imaṁ khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, ādīnavaṁ disvā evaṁ vadāmi.
sn35.235:5.1 Varaṁ, bhikkhave, tiṇhāya sattiyā ādittāya sampajjalitāya sajotibhūtāya kāyindriyaṁ sampalimaṭṭhaṁ, na tveva kāyaviññeyyesu phoṭṭhabbesu anubyañjanaso nimittaggāho.
sn35.235:5.2 Nimittassādagathitaṁ vā, bhikkhave, viññāṇaṁ tiṭṭhamānaṁ tiṭṭheyya, anubyañjanassādagathitaṁ vā tasmiñce samaye kālaṁ kareyya.
sn35.235:5.3 Ṭhānametaṁ vijjati, yaṁ dvinnaṁ gatīnaṁ aññataraṁ gatiṁ gaccheyya—
sn35.235:5.4 nirayaṁ vā tiracchānayoniṁ vā.
sn35.235:5.5 Imaṁ khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, ādīnavaṁ disvā evaṁ vadāmi.
sn35.235:6.1 Varaṁ, bhikkhave, sottaṁ.
sn35.235:6.2 Sottaṁ kho panāhaṁ, bhikkhave, vañjhaṁ jīvitānaṁ vadāmi, aphalaṁ jīvitānaṁ vadāmi, momūhaṁ jīvitānaṁ vadāmi, na tveva tathārūpe vitakke vitakkeyya yathārūpānaṁ vitakkānaṁ vasaṁ gato saṅghaṁ bhindeyya.
sn35.235:6.3 Imaṁ khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, vañjhaṁ jīvitānaṁ ādīnavaṁ disvā evaṁ vadāmi.
sn35.235:7.1 Tattha, bhikkhave, sutavā ariyasāvako iti paṭisañcikkhati:
sn35.235:7.2 ‘tiṭṭhatu tāva tattāya ayosalākāya ādittāya sampajjalitāya sajotibhūtāya cakkhundriyaṁ sampalimaṭṭhaṁ.
sn35.235:7.3 Handāhaṁ idameva manasi karomi—
sn35.235:7.4 iti cakkhu aniccaṁ, rūpā aniccā, cakkhuviññāṇaṁ aniccaṁ, cakkhusamphasso anicco, yampidaṁ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi aniccaṁ’.
sn35.235:8.1 Tiṭṭhatu tāva tiṇhena ayosaṅkunā ādittena sampajjalitena sajotibhūtena sotindriyaṁ sampalimaṭṭhaṁ.
sn35.235:8.2 Handāhaṁ idameva manasi karomi—
sn35.235:8.3 iti sotaṁ aniccaṁ, saddā aniccā, sotaviññāṇaṁ aniccaṁ, sotasamphasso anicco, yampidaṁ sotasamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi aniccaṁ.
sn35.235:9.1 Tiṭṭhatu tāva tiṇhena nakhacchedanena ādittena sampajjalitena sajotibhūtena ghānindriyaṁ sampalimaṭṭhaṁ.
sn35.235:9.2 Handāhaṁ idameva manasi karomi—
sn35.235:9.3 iti ghānaṁ aniccaṁ, gandhā aniccā, ghānaviññāṇaṁ aniccaṁ, ghānasamphasso anicco, yampidaṁ ghānasamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ …pe… tampi aniccaṁ.
sn35.235:10.1 Tiṭṭhatu tāva tiṇhena khurena ādittena sampajjalitena sajotibhūtena jivhindriyaṁ sampalimaṭṭhaṁ.
sn35.235:10.2 Handāhaṁ idameva manasi karomi—
sn35.235:10.3 iti jivhā aniccā, rasā aniccā, jivhāviññāṇaṁ aniccaṁ, jivhāsamphasso anicco, yampidaṁ jivhāsamphassapaccayā uppajjati …pe… tampi aniccaṁ.
sn35.235:11.1 Tiṭṭhatu tāva tiṇhāya sattiyā ādittāya sampajjalitāya sajotibhūtāya kāyindriyaṁ sampalimaṭṭhaṁ.
sn35.235:11.2 Handāhaṁ idameva manasi karomi—
sn35.235:11.3 iti kāyo anicco, phoṭṭhabbā aniccā, kāyaviññāṇaṁ aniccaṁ, kāyasamphasso anicco, yampidaṁ kāyasamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ …pe… tampi aniccaṁ.
sn35.235:12.1 Tiṭṭhatu tāva sottaṁ.
sn35.235:12.2 Handāhaṁ idameva manasi karomi—
sn35.235:12.3 iti mano anicco, dhammā aniccā, manoviññāṇaṁ aniccaṁ, manosamphasso anicco, yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tampi aniccaṁ”.
sn35.235:13.1 Evaṁ passaṁ, bhikkhave, sutavā ariyasāvako cakkhusmimpi nibbindati, rūpesupi nibbindati, cakkhuviññāṇepi nibbindati, cakkhusamphassepi nibbindati …pe…
sn35.235:13.2 yampidaṁ manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṁ sukhaṁ vā dukkhaṁ vā adukkhamasukhaṁ vā tasmimpi nibbindati.
sn35.235:13.3 Nibbindaṁ virajjati; virāgā vimuccati; vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti.
sn35.235:13.4 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānāti.
sn35.235:13.5 Ayaṁ kho, bhikkhave, ādittapariyāyo, dhammapariyāyo”ti.
sn35.235:13.6 Aṭṭhamaṁ. "

sn35.236:0.2 18. Samuddavagga
sn35.236:0.3 Paṭhamahatthapādopamasutta
sn35.236:1.1 “Hatthesu, bhikkhave, sati ādānanikkhepanaṁ paññāyati;
sn35.236:1.2 pādesu sati abhikkamapaṭikkamo paññāyati;
sn35.236:1.3 pabbesu sati samiñjanapasāraṇaṁ paññāyati;
sn35.236:1.4 kucchismiṁ sati jighacchā pipāsā paññāyati.
sn35.236:1.5 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, cakkhusmiṁ sati cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati ajjhattaṁ sukhaṁ dukkhaṁ …pe…
sn35.236:1.6 jivhāya sati jivhāsamphassapaccayā uppajjati ajjhattaṁ sukhaṁ dukkhaṁ …pe…
sn35.236:1.7 manasmiṁ sati manosamphassapaccayā uppajjati ajjhattaṁ sukhaṁ dukkhaṁ …pe….
sn35.236:2.1 Hatthesu, bhikkhave, asati ādānanikkhepanaṁ na paññāyati;
sn35.236:2.2 pādesu asati abhikkamapaṭikkamo na paññāyati;
sn35.236:2.3 pabbesu asati samiñjanapasāraṇaṁ na paññāyati;
sn35.236:2.4 kucchismiṁ asati jighacchā pipāsā na paññāyati.
sn35.236:2.5 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, cakkhusmiṁ asati cakkhusamphassapaccayā nuppajjati ajjhattaṁ sukhaṁ dukkhaṁ …pe…
sn35.236:2.6 jivhāya asati jivhāsamphassapaccayā nuppajjati …pe…
sn35.236:2.7 manasmiṁ asati manosamphassapaccayā nuppajjati ajjhattaṁ sukhaṁ dukkhan”ti.

sn35.237:2.2 pādesu asati abhikkamapaṭikkamo na hoti;
